pramāṇa tā vyāpti ādi sattvāt anyathā pramāṇe nairapekṣasya vaiyarthyāt  na ca ācāre veda mūlatva prasiddheḥ tad anumānam asiddheḥ vyabhicārāt anyathā upapatteḥ ca na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigrahāt tathā na hi veda mūlaḥ  ayam iti kṛtvā mahājanānām tad parigrahaḥ veda mūla tvasya prathamam jñātum aśakyatvāt śakya tve vā kim anumānena na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigṛhītaḥ  ayam ācāra iti jñātvā tatra mahā jana parigrahaḥ gauravāt asiddheḥ ca pūrva mahā jana parigrahāt eva uttarottareṣām parigrahāt anuṣṭhāna upapatteḥ tādṛśa smṛti ācārayoḥ veda mala tvena vyāpteḥ veda siddhiḥ iti ced  na asambhavat mūla antara tvasya upādhi tvāt anyathā lobha nyāya mūla smṛteḥ api veda mūlatva prasaṅgaḥ astu vā smṛti ācārayoḥ anādi tvam na ca ācārāt  smṛtiḥ smṛteḥ ācāra iti andha paramparā mūla bhūta pramāṇa abhāvāt iti vacyam smṛti ācārayoḥ ubhayoḥ api pramāṇa tvāt  anyathā na tatas  veda anumānam api iti ucyate pralaye pūrva smṛti ācārayoḥ ucchedāt sarga ādau nitya sarvajñeśvara praṇīta veda mūla tvam smṛti ācārayoḥ anyathā mūla abhāvena andha paramparā prasaṅgaḥ na ca manu ādīnām atīndriya artha darśi tvam tad upāya śravaṇa ādeḥ tadānīm abhavāt  pūrva sarga siddha sarvajñam anvādaya eva te iti ced  na pramāṇa abhāvāt  smṛti ācārayoḥ pramāṇa mūla tvam eva tad kalpanam iti ced  na pratisargam teṣām anyonyatva kalpane gauravam iti ekasya eva nitya sarvajñasya kalpanāt  na ca smṛtaya eva tad praṇītāḥ tāsām manu ādi kartṛka tvena smṛtau bodhanāt  smṛtau  eva smṛtīnām veda mūlatva smaraṇāñca evañca smṛti ācārayoḥ mahājana parigrahāt veda mūlatva sādhakam api bhagavati pramāṇam ata eva pratimanvantarañcā eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate iti āgamaḥ  api evañca pūrvam pratyakṣa mūlau  eva smṛti ācārau agre ca kāla krameṇa āyuḥ ārogya bala śraddhā grahaṇa dhāraṇa ādi śakteḥ aharapacīyamāna tvāt tad adhyayana vicchedana śākhā ucchedāt  smṛti ācārabhyām eva kartavyatām adhigatya pravṛttiḥ nanu evam smṛtiḥ astu veda mūlā maṅgala ādi ācāraḥ tu īśvarāt eva bhaviṣyati ghaṭa lipya ādi samprādayavat iti ced  na bahu vyāpāra ghaṭitasya tad tad ācārasya guru tvena maṅgalam ācaret ityādi vākyasya eva lāghavena kalpanāt  na ca maṅgala ādi pada śakti graha arthe tad upapatteḥ ata eva yatra vacana mātrāt  para pratipattiḥ tatra na ācāraḥ parīkṣakāṇām tasya ca veda tvam na īśvara praṇīta tvena śakti grahaṇa artha tad vacane vyabhicārāt  kintu tādṛśa ācāra asya veda mūlatva niyamāt iti syāt et  pralaye sati evam eva tad  sa eva tu na asti pramāṇa abhāvat iti ced  na kāla kapālāni āvṛtti ghaṭa prāgabhāvaḥ kārya dravya an ādhāra ādhāraḥ kārya dravya an adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛttiḥ vā abhāva tvāt  ākāśa vṛtti anyonya abhāvavat iti vṛtta pralaya sādhanāt  evam eva ghaṭa dhvaṃsam pakṣīkṛtya āgāmi pralaya sādhanam yad vā ghaṭaḥ kārya dravya an adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt śabdavat  yad vā kārya dravya tvam kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogi vṛtti kārya mātra vṛtti tvāt śabda tvavat  yad vā eka kālīnāḥ sarve paramāṇavaḥ samagrīpādeya prabandha śūnyā ārambhaka tvāt  naṣṭa pavana ārambhaka paramāṇuvat  sarvatra pakṣa tā avacchedaka avacchinnam sādhyam pratīyate iti eka kāle śūnyate labhyate na ca pavana paramāṇūnām api pakṣa tvena aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam pakṣa dharmatā bala labhya sādhya apratīteḥ abheda anumānavat ca pakṣasya dṛṣṭāntatva avirodhaḥ yad vā paramāṇavaḥ kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa vṛtti kāryavantaḥ nitya dravya tvāt ākāśavat  bhū golaka santānaḥ  ayam bhū golaka santānānadhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt  ghaṭavat  yad vā etad karma atiktāni karmāṇi etad pratibandhaka pratibadhyāni karma tvāt  etad karmavat  na ca atra vyabhicāra śaṅkā sarveṣām evaṃrūpa tvāt anevambhāve ca svabhāva pracyavāt anyathā niyame api niyama antara apekṣāyām anavasthiteḥ āgamaḥ  api amum ā iva artham saṃvata di iti kṛtam prasakta anuprasaktyā vidhivāda pūrva pakṣaḥ ācāra mūla tvam vedasya pravartaka jñāna janaka tvena bhavati iti pravartaka jñānam nirūpyate tatra abhidhā saṅkalpa apūrva bhāvanā jñānam na pravartakam tasmin sati api apravṛtteḥ asatī api pravṛtteḥ ca kāryatva jñānam pravartakam iti guravaḥ tathā hi jñānasya kṛtau janyāyām cikīrṣā atiriktam na kartavyam asti tad sattve kṛti vilambaḥ hetu antara abhāvāt cikīrṣā ca kṛti sādhyatva prakārikā kṛti sādhya kriyā viṣaya icchā pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti tad anubhavāt sā ca sva kṛti sādhya tā jñāna sādhyā icchāyāḥ sva prakāraka dhī sādhyatva niyamāt ata eva sva kṛti sādhye pāke pravartate na tu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyā sva kṛtya sadhye cikīrṣā patteḥ sva kṛti asādhyatva jñānam pratibandhakam iti ced  na tad abhāva kāraṇa tve gauravāt  atha abhāva ubhaya siddhaḥ kṛti sādhya ta adhīra siddha ityatas  na lāghava avasara iti ced  na yatra śabdāt anumāna dvā daivāt  sā tatra lāghava avatārāt i  chāyāḥ sva prakāraka jñāna sādhyatva niyamena kṛti sādhyatva jñānasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca janaka jñānam vighaṭayata eva jñānasya pratibandhaka tvāt ca vyāpti jñāna vighaṭana dvārā anumiti pratibandhaka anaikāntika jñānavat anyathā sva kṛti asādhyatva aniṣṭa sādhanatva upekṣaṇītva niṣphalatva jñānam pratibandhakam kriyā jñānam eva pravartakam kalpeta nanu sanaḥ dhātu artha gocara icchā vāci tvāt lāghavāñca kṛtau  icchā cikīrṣā sā ca vṛṣṭauviva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt iti ced  na vahninā sādhayāmi itivat  kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchāyāḥ kṛteḥ pūrvam anubhūyamānāyāḥ sanantā vācya tvena gauraveṇa ca pratyākhyātum aśakyatvāt  kiñca pākam cikīrṣati iti atra prādhānyena pākasya icchā viṣaya tvam anubhūyate na tu kṛteḥ dhātoḥ ca san pratyaya abhidheya icchā prakāra vāci tvam odanam bubhukṣata iti atra bhojana viśeṣya tayā odanasya icchā viṣayatva anubhavāt iṣṭa sādhana tvena vṛṣṭau  iva kṛtau  icchā sambhave api kṛti icchā na pravartikā kintu sva kṛti sādhya icśā eva ghaṭam jānāti cikīrṣati karotī jñāna cikīrṣā kṛtīnām eka viṣayatva anubhavāt atha yadi kṛtyā sādhayitum icchā sā tadā cikīrṣitasya pākasya anyatas  siddhau sā na apagacchet na hi upāya viśeṣa sādhya tvena icchā upāya antara adhīna phala lābhena nivāryate prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsāyāḥ  anivṛtteḥ iti ced  na sva viṣaya siddha tvasya phala icchā vicchedasya ca upāya icchā virodha tvāt  asti ca tatra pāka odanayoḥ siddha tvam anya odana icchāyām pāka cikīrṣā bhavati eva pratyuta asiddha tvāt kṛtau  eva icchā na vicchidyeta yadi kṛti viṣaya siddhatva phala icchā vicchedau na virodhinau prītyā dhana lābhe ca tad adhika dhana icchā na vicchidyate tasya asiddha tvāt tad phala icchāyāḥ ca sattvāt  dhana mātra arthinaḥ ca prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsā na asti eva dhana mātrasya siddha tvāt  kiñcid viśeṣa siddhyā eva hi sāmānya it chā vicchedaḥ anyathā sakala sva viṣaya siddheḥ asambhavena tad vicchedaḥ  na syāt eva vastutas tu kriyā anukūlā kṛtiḥ iṣṭa upāya iti jñāne kriyāyāḥ kṛti sādhya tvam iṣṭa upāya tvañca bhātam kriyā dvāra eva kṛteḥ iṣṭa sādhana tvāt iti tad bodhāt  kṛtau  iva kṛti sādhya tvena kriyāyām api sā eva icchā iti cikīrṣāyām kṛti sādhyatva prakāra naiyatyamatas  kṛti samāna viṣaya cikīrṣā tvena cikīrṣāyāḥ kṛti kāraṇa tvam na tu kṛti icchā tvena bhinna viṣaya tayā gauravāt  tathā api yena rūpeṇa yasya iṣṭa sādhana tvam tena prakāreṇa tatra icchā yathā sva kedāra vṛṣṭi tvena iṣṭa sādhana tvāt  tathā eva aicchā tathā kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvam atas  kṛti sādhya tvena tatra icchā bhavati iti kṛtau kṛti viṣaye vā cikīrṣāyām na vṛṣṭī icchā vilakṣaṇa sāmagrayantara kalpanam iti ced  bhavet evam yadi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā syāt  na ca evam gauravāt  kintu pāka tvena sa tu kṛtim vinā na iti anyat etad vahninā sādhayāmi itivat  kṛtyā sādhayā ami iti icchā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt eva iti ced  tarhi tatra vahni sādhya tā jñānavat atra api kṛti sādhyatva jñānam kāraṇam āvaśyakam kṛtau ca anubhava siddha cikīrṣā adhīnata tvam viśeṣaḥ tena prāṇa pañcaka sañcāre jīvana yoni kṛti sādhye na pravṛttiḥ anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tatra pravarteta nanu cikīrṣā adhīna tvasya upalakṣaṇa tve upalakṣya mātra gata anati prasakta dharma abhāvāt kṛti mātrasya ca atiprasaṅgāt  tad tad kṛti viśeṣā upalakṣyāḥ tathā ca tad ananugamāt pravṛtti ananugamaḥ viśeṣaṇa tve cikīrṣāyām pravṛttau ca cikīrṣā jñāna kāraṇa tve gauravam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ca kiñca cikīrṣā asādhya avasthāyāḥ kṛteḥ siddha avastha sādhanatva virodhena kṛti sādhya tā pāka ādau na jñāyeta iti ced  na asti hi kṛti viśeṣaḥ mānasa pratyakṣa siddhaḥ jīvana yoni prayatna vyāvṛttaḥ cikīrṣā upalakṣyaḥ yatra cikīrṣā kāraṇatva grahaḥ sa ca tava jāti rūpaḥ  mama tu anugata kāraṇa upādhi rūpaḥ evañca cikīrṣā adhīna tvena anugatena kṛti viśeṣāṇām upalakṣyāṇām anugata tvam api yathā gaḥ tveṇa taṭa sthe na upalakṣitā mahiṣī ādi vyāvṛtta dhāna karma vyakti viśeṣāḥ dhenupadena ucyate na tu gaḥ tvam api tathā cikīrṣā api evam jīvana yoni yatna vyāvṛtta kṛti viśeṣāṇām kṛti tvena jñānam kāraṇam iti na ananugamaḥ nanu kṛti sādhye na kṛtiḥ viśeṣaṇam asattvāt  sattve vā kṛtau satyām jñānam jñāne ca kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ na upalakṣaṇam ati prasaṅgāt iti ced  na kṛtiḥ hi jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam eva sādhye ca paricāyaka tayā upalakṣaṇam anyathā iṣṭa sādhane api iṣṭam na viśeṣaṇam asattvāt  na upalakṣaṇa m ati prasaṅgāt liṅga jñāna ādau vā kā gatiḥ nanu evam śrame api cikīrṣā syāt tasya api cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti sādhya tvāt atra vadanti śramaḥ tu bhojana ādi kriyā asādhyaḥ  na tad kṛti sādhyaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt  kṛteḥ sva dhvaṃsa sākṣātkāra atirikte cikīrṣā viṣaya mātre janakatvāt  na hi bhojana cikīrṣā viṣaya mātre janakatvāt  na hi bhojana cikīrṣā adhīna kṛtyā gamanam sādhyate iti kecid  tad na gurutara bhāra uttolane kṛtya sādhye bhramāt  pravṛttasya nigaḍa niścala dehasya vā kṛtau satyām uttolana calana kriyā anutpāde api śrama anubhavāt  kṛteḥ eva kāraṇa tvāt  na tu tad janya kriyāyāḥ sukhe vyabhicārāt ca na hi sukham kṛti kāraṇa cikīrṣā viṣayaḥ upāya cikīrṣā janyā hi kṛtiḥ na tu sukha cikīrṣā janyā cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam na śrame dveṣa yoni prayatnāt api tad utpatteḥ iti apare tad na śatru badhasya iṣṭa sā ādhatana tvena cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvāt dveṣasya yatna ajanaka tvāt  dveṣa siddhiḥ tu śatrum dveṣmi iti anubhava balāt yad tu śramaḥ kṛti tvena kṛti sādhyaḥ  na cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti tvena yadi acikīrṣi atepi śrame cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti tvena kāraṇa tā syāt  tadā cikīrṣitam eva bhojanam kṛtyā sādhyate na acikīrṣitam gamana ādi iti na syāt  śrama vaṅgamane api tad janyatva prasaṅgāt  bhojana ādiḥ ca cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti viśeṣāt sa hi kṛti mātram vyabhicārati jīvana yokṛteḥ tad anutpādāt  yad vā śramaḥ  na bhojana kṛti sādhyaḥ kintu tad nirantara utpannat jīvana yoni prayatnāt eva iti tad na na hi kṛti tvena tad śrama janaka tvam na api kṛti antarāt eva śrama utpattiḥ jīvana yoni prayatne sati api bhāra udvahana ādikam akurvataḥ tādṛśa namān anubhavena tasya śrama ajanaka tvāt  tasmāt  bhojana ādivat  śrama viśeṣaṇām api bhojana ādi kṛti sādhya tvam ananya gatika tvāt suptasya sveda ādi anumitaḥ śramaḥ tad janya iti ced  na sveda ādeḥ śramāni ahetuka tvāt anyathā jāgare api tad anuvṛttau śrama anuvṛtti prasaṅgāt  iti mā evam sva icchā adhīna kṛti śeṣaṇa tvāt śramaḥ ca niyamataḥ  anya icśā adhīna kṛti sādhyaḥ śrame duḥkha tvena icchā virahāt  ata eva anya icchā janya kṛti sādhya tvena śramaḥ  na antarīyaka iti ucyate sva cikīrṣa adhīna tvantu na kṛtau viśeṣaṇam gauravāt  anye tu kṛti gatam dharma antaram eva uddeśya tvam tad viśiṣṭa kṛti sādhyaḥ ca na śramaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt  kintu kṛti mātra sādhyaḥ ata eva kaṣṭam karma iti anubhavaḥ lokānām evam cikīrṣāyām mama ekam kṛti sādhya tvam prayojakam tava tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañca iti catuṣṭayam icchā prayoja kantu mama sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañca iti dvayam vṛṣṭi sādhna tvena tatra icchā sādhana tvasya icchā virodhi tvāt  tava tu cayam viṣa bhakṣaṇe tu kṛti sādhya tve api balavat aniṣṭa sādhana tvena cikīrṣā na asti iti kṛtau cikīrṣā janya tvam viśeṣaṇam iti kaścid  tad tuccham evam hi viṣa bhakṣaṇam kṛti sādhyam eva na syāt  jīvana yoni kṛte stasya anutpatteḥ iti vyartham viśeṣaṇam syāt etad  iṣṭa sādhana tā bhramāt  viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam asti jñāna prayukta tvāt  kāryatvasya tathā ca sañjāta bādhaḥ api tatra kāryam tu ajñānāt pravarteta tathā tṛptaḥ  api bhojane nanu sva kṛti sādhyata anubhavaḥ tathā anyathā iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇe viṣa bhakṣaṇe api pravarteta na ceṣṭa sā adhana tā jñānam vedaḥ vā anubhāvakam asti iti ced  na vastutas tatra kṛti sādhya tve liṅga antareṇa āpta vākyena vā tad anubhava sambhavāt liṅga ābhāsāt śabda ābhāsāt vā apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca bheda agrahavādinaḥ tad ca tava tad anubhava abhāvāt mā evam sva viśeṣaṇavat tā pratisandhāna janyam hi kārya tā jñānam pravartakam tathā hi kāmye puruṣa viśeṣaṇam kāmanā tatas  kāmya sādhana tā jñānena yāga pāka ādau kārya tā jñānam nitye ca kāla śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇam tathā ca etad sandhyāyām aham kṛti sādhya saṃdhyā vandanaḥ saṃdhyā samaye śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam tad uktam sa ca kārya viśeṣaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaṇa avagataḥ pravṛtti hetuḥ iti saṃjāta bādhasya ca viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca bhramadaśāyām iva na iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam asti yena tad janya kārya tā jñānāt pravarteta tṛptasya ca kāmanā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna abhāva na tathā bodhaḥ anye tu ātmanaḥ  jīvitva pratisandhāna janyam śrame kṛti sādhya tā jñānam sambhavati iti jīvana vyatirikta tvam sva viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇam iti tad na śrame sva icchā dhīna kṛti sādhyatva abhāvāt iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakam kārya tā jñānam pravartakam iti apare tad na nitye tad abhāvāt nanu viṣa bhakṣaṇa vyāvṛttam iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva kṛti sādhyatā jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam astu sva viśeṣaṇavat tā jñāna janyatva apekṣayā laghu tvāt  kiñca upāya viṣayā cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyā upāya icchā tvāt  vṛṣṭī icchāvat  bhoga cikīrṣāyām tad abhāvau  aprayojakam iṣṭa sādhana tvam iti ced  na tava api sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janyatva abhāvena tatra tasya aprayojaka tvāt  kṛti hetu cikīrṣāyām tad  prayojakam na ca bhoga cikīrṣā tathā upāya cikīrṣāta eva kṛti sambhavāt  iti ced  tulyam iti mā evam sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhena ekatra jñātum aśakyatvāt  asiddha avasthasya hi sādhya tvam siddha tādaśāyām tad abhāvāt siddha tādaśā āyāñca sādhana tvam asiddha avasthāvataḥ kārya anutpatteḥ tathā ca pāka ādeḥ asiddhatva siddhatva jñāne sādhyatva sādhana tvagrahaḥ na ca ekam ekena ekadā siddha mama siddhañca iti jñāyate na ca sva rūpa gatatā sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ atas  na virodha iti vācyam yadi hi svarūpa nibandhanam tad ubhayam tadā tad svarūpam sadā eva siddham asiddhañca syāt  bhinna nirūpita tve api tayoḥ siddhatva asiddhatve anavagamya ajñānāt tasmāt  samaya bheda upādhika eva tad ubhaya sambandhaḥ pāke idānīm sādhya tvam agre sādhana tvam jñāyata iti ced  na idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt ananugamena vyāpti agrahāt śabdena tathā pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt  gauravāt ca na ca kṛtitaḥ siddham iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt  cikīrṣā na hi siddham kaścid  cikīrṣati kṛteḥ pūrva kṛtitaḥ siddham iti jñāna abhavāt ca na ca kṛti sādhya tvena pāka ādeḥ iṣṭa sādhatvāt  sādhana tvam api sādhyam na hi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā iti uktam tasmāt  kṛta kriyamāṇa vilakṣaṇam kṛti anantara bhaviṣyattā rūpam kṛti sādhya tvam cikīrṣā prayojakam tādṛśañca sādhanatva virodhi ā iva kiñca sādhana tvasya siddha mātra dharma tvāt sādhanatva jñānam icchā virodhi na hi kaścid  siddham icchati iti uktam etena vṛṣṭi ādau  iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena kḷptam iti nirastam katham tarhi svatas  asundare vṛṣṭi ādi vicchā tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt iti gṛhāṇa anye tu sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana iṣṭi  chā prayojakam anugatam uddeśya tvam puruṣa artha pada vedanīyam dharma antaram asti anugata kāryasya anugata kāraṇa niyamya tvāt tad eva duḥkha tad sādhana ādau cikīrṣā prayojakam iti na ca duḥkha virodhi tvam eva tathā asti iti vācyam saha anavasthāna niyama virodhasya asambhavāt badhyadhātaka bhāvasya eka samaye samāna adhikaraṇyā bhāvasya ca yatna ādi sādhāraṇyāt iti tad na tad ajñāne api sukhatva jñānāt icchotpatteḥ na hi sukha tve jñāte dharma antara jñānam vinā na icchati tathā tve svatas  prayojana hāni āpatteḥ tad eva hi svatas  prayojanam tad avagatam sat  sva vṛttitayā iṣyate kiñca anugata dharma kalpanā api kāraṇe na ca sukha ādi icchā karaṇam anāgata tvāt  kintu tad avagamaḥ tarhi sukha ādi jñāne tad  sva rūpa sadeva icchā prayojakam astu iti ced  na yathā hi uddeśya tvam sukha jñāna ādiṣu utpadyate anyatara tvāt  tṛṇa araṇi maṇi nyāyāt vā tathā eva icchā eva jāyatām kṛti sādhyatvañca kṛtau satyām agri makṣaṇe svarūpam na kṛtim vinā kṣema sādhāraṇañca etad  kṛti sādhyatvañca na kṛteḥ pūrvam nanu kṛtau naṣṭāyām san  api dharmī na kāryaḥ tathā ca katham kārye apūrve kāminaḥ  anvayaḥ kṣaṇika tvena kriyā tulya tvāt iti ced  na yad vṛtti kāmya sādhana tvam tatra kārya tā buddheḥ prayojaka tvāt  na tu kārya tā viśiṣṭasya kāmya sādhana tā iti vyāptiḥ nanu pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tā jñānam na pratyakṣeṇa kṛti anantaram pāke sati kṛti sādhya tā jñānam tasmin sati kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayāt kṛti sādhya totīrṇe cikīrṣā akṛtya uḥ asambhavāt ca iti ced  na pākaḥ  mad kṛti sādhyaḥ mad kṛtim vinā asattve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt  daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt vā mad bhojanavat iti anumānāt  sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam yasya yad iṣṭa sādhanam yad kṛtim vinā yadā na sambhavati tad  tadā tad kati sādhyam iti vyāpteḥ asiddhasya iṣṭa sā dhanatva abhāvāt balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvañca liṅga viśeṣaṇam tena na madhu viṣa saṃmpṛkta anna bhojane vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyatas tasya api kṛti sādhya totīrṇe na vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyatas tasya api kṛti sādhya tvāt  atīta tā daśā yāñca atīta odana icchā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhanatva abhāvāt ata eva nidāgha dūna deha uvarṣati vāri de toyadā toya lābha sambhāvanāyām vā saraḥ  avagāhane na pravartate iṣṭa santāpa śānti sādhana toya sambandhasya sva kṛtim vinā api siddhi pratisandhānena liṅga abhāvena sva kṛti sādhyatva jñāna abhāvāt yadā ca mad kṛtim vinā na sambhavati iti pratisandhatte tadā pravartate yasya santāpa śāntim mātram iṣṭam sa sataḥ  avagāhanasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvam eva na pratisandhatte upasthita vṛṣṭitaḥ  api tad sambhavāt iti kaścid  tad na toya sambandha tvena santāpa śānti sādhana tvam tasya ca saraḥ  avagāhane api sattvāt  anyathā vṛṣṭiḥ api tad sādhanam na syāt  saraḥ  avagāhanāt api tad siddheḥ kārya sādhanatvañca kṛti sādhya tve na liṅgam pāka ādivat odana ādeḥ api pravṛtteḥ pūrvam kṛti sādhyatva jñāne hetu abhāvāt  nanu evam liṅga jñānam eva pravartakam astu prāthamika tvāt  āvaśyaka tvān ca na ca lāghavāt  kṛti sādhyatva jñānam tathā kṛti sādhyata anumitau tadā māna abhāvena yugapad upasthiti abhāvāt pravṛtti sāmagṣa anumiti pravibandhāñca iti ced  na liṅga jñāne kṛti sādhyatva aprakāśe tad prakāraka cikīrṣāyām tasya ahetu tvāt ata eva liṅga antara jñānam api na pravartakam nanu pāka ādiḥ kṛtaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ vā na pakṣaḥ tasya kṛti sādhya tve bādhāt  na api anāgataḥ bhāvi pāke māna abhāvena āśraya asiddheḥ pāka tvam bhaviṣyat vṛtti sāmānya tvāt  gaḥ tvavat  iti mānam iti ced  na māna abhāvena gaḥ tve api tasya aprasiddheḥ pāka mātram pakṣa iti ced  na mātrā arthaḥ  yadi pāka tvam tadā bādholiṅgā siddhiḥ ca sarva pāka paratve ca tasya siddha bhāge bādhaḥ  anāgata bhāge ca āśraya asiddhiḥ vartamāna ādi udāsīnaḥ pākaḥ pakṣaḥ pāka sāmānye ca kṛti sādhya tvam na bādhitam iti api na siddhasya pakṣa tvam na asiddhasya iti anumiteḥ siddha viṣaya tve bādhāt  bhinna viṣaya tve vā siddha viṣaya icchā pravṛtti ādi anutpādaka tvāt ca kṛta kriyamāṇa sādhāraṇa kṛti sādhyatva jñānāt eva asiddha viṣayā cikīrṣā kṛtiḥ ca utpadyate ananya gatika tvena tathā kāraṇa svabhāva kalpanāt iti ced  tarhi yādṛśam kṛti sādhya tvam cikīrṣāyām prakāraḥ tādṛśam jñāne na asti iti anya prakāraka jñānāt eva cikīrṣā syāt  tathā ca liṅga jñānam eva pravṛtti hetuḥ astu prāthamika tvāt  yad tu smṛta pāke kṛti sādhyatva asaṃsargā grahāt pravṛttiḥ sa ca asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā grahāt iti tad na smṛta pākasya siddha tvena tatra kāryatva asaṃsarga grahe anumāna bādhāt  smṛta pākasya siddha tvam tadā na gṛhyate iti ced  tarhi smṛta pākasya siddha tvagrahe odana arthī pāke na pravarteta tatra pāka ādau siddhatva grahāt tad asaṃsarga graha iti cetulyam api ca smṛta pāke kāryatva asaṃsargāt vidyamānā saṃsarga āgrahāt visaṃvādinī pravṛttiḥ syāt  kiñca evam siddha pāka jñānāt ajñāte asiddhe pāke icchā pravṛttī syātām iti atra brūmaḥ pāke kṛti sādhya tvam siddha t siddhe bādhāt  anāgata pākam ādāya sidhyati pakṣa tā avacchedaka dharma sāmānādhikaraṇyam sādhyamānasya liṅgena sidhyati iti anumāne kḷtvāt  yathā prasiddha vahni bādhe api vahni mātram na bādhitam iti aprasiddhaḥ  api vahniḥ sidhyati tathā prasiddha pāke kṛti sādhyatva bādhe api pāka mātre na bādhitam iti aprasiddham pākam ādāya tad sidhyati aprasiddhayoḥ pakṣa sādhyayoḥ siddhau  aviśeṣāt tasmāt  asiddhasya kvacid  siddhe siddhe siddhasya ca kvacid  aprasiddhasya ca asiddhe siddhiḥ tena anumā tridhā anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tvam katham avagamyeta kiñca tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt katham vṛṣṭi ādau  icchā siddhatvasya icchā virodhi tvāt  anāgatasya jñātum aśakyatvāt  ata eva siddha asiddha viṣayatva nirāsena sukha ādi jñānāt phale api na iccha iti na vṛṣṭyādāviṣṭa sādhana tā api na ca vṛṣṭi ādi sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vṛṣṭi ādau  icchā icchāyāḥ siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣayatva vikalpa grāsāt atha sāmānya lakṣaṇa pratyāsattyā vṛṣṭi ādi tvena sukha ādi tvena ca siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣaya kam jñānam utpannam tena siddham virodhinam tyaktva asiddha viṣaya icchā utpadyate yadi ca sāmānya lakṣaṇā na asti tadā yena rūpeṇa iṣṭa sā adhanatva grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa jñāte siddhe vecchā utpadyate anvaya vyatirekābhyām tādṛśa jñānasya tādṛśa icchā janakatva avadhāraṇāt sukha icchāyām api ekam iti ced  tarhi mama api pāka tvāt chedena kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt anāgate cikīrṣā tad ca jñānam sakala pāka viṣayam sannikṛṣṭa pāka viṣayam vā iti anyat etad bālasya vyāpti ādi graheṇa ādyā pravṛttiḥ jīvana adṛṣṭa udbodhita janma antara saṃskāra janyāt stana pānam kāryam iti smaraṇāt  tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇāt  tatra pravṛttiḥ ananya gatika tvāt  na ca janmāntare api paryanuyogaḥ janma dhārāyāḥ  anādi tvāt  pratyakṣa anumāna mūlaka tvāt ca na andha paramparā vastutas tu śuṣka kaṇṭha tayā bālaḥ  duḥkham anubhavan virodhitayā sukham smarati tatas  sukhatva jñānāt  sukha vṛtti kārya tvam sukha vṛtti tayā antaraṅga tvāt na tu stana pānam iṣṭa sādhanam iti smaraṇam sukha āvṛtti tvena vahiḥ aṅga tvāt  sukha kāryatvañca stana pānam api viṣayaḥ tena stana pāne kāryatva jñānāt eva pravṛttiḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya tadānīm sāmāgṣa bhāvāt  evañca ādya pravṛttau kāryatva jñānam prayojakam kḷptam iti agre api tad eva pravartakam kḷpta tvāt  navīnāstu mama idam kṛti sādhyam iti jñānam na pravartakam anāgata viṣaye pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ asambhavāt  kintu yādṛśasya puruṣasya kṛti sādhyam yad dṛṣṭam tādṛśa tvam ātmanaḥ pratisandhāya tatra pravartate tathā hi odana kāmasya tad sādhana tā jñānavataḥ ca taṇḍula ādi upakaraṇavataḥ pākaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ aham api ca tādṛśa iti jñānāt  pāke pravartate evañcānya kṛta pāke kṛti sādhya tā jñānam ātmanaḥ pāke kṛti sādhyatva prayojaka viśeṣaṇavattva jñānañca prapartakam anyatra api pravṛttiḥ evam eva iti anāditā eva ata eva sañcāta bādhaḥ caitya vandane viṣaya bhakṣaṇe ca na pravartate iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavataḥ  hi tad  kṛti sādhyam na ca sañjāta bādhaḥ tatra iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavān evam tṛpti icchāvataḥ  api bhojanam kṛti sādhyam tṛptaḥ ca na tṛpti icchāvat tvam ātmani ava iti iti na bhojane pravartate ati navīnāḥ tu yādṛśasya ityādau avigīta tvam tad kṛtau viśeṣaṇam āhuḥ sañjāta bādhaḥ tu viṣa bhakṣaṇam caitya vandanañca vigīta kṛtita adhya tvena eva jānāti iti tatra na pravartate pravṛtti viṣayaḥ ca sāmānyatas  kāla asambhinnaḥ pāka ādiḥ jñāyate pravṛtti mahimnā ca anāgata pāka siddhiḥ cikīrṣā ca kāla asambhinna viṣayā na tu bhāvinam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti ākārā eva iti vidhivāda siddhāntaḥ atra ucyate viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādi vyāvṛttam kṛti sādhyatva jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam viṣaya tayā avacchedakam lāghavāt  na tu sva viśeṣaṇavat tā pratisandhāna janya tvam gauravāt  na ca siddha asiddha avasthayoḥ sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ nirviśeṣitayoḥ tayoḥ avirodhāt pākaḥ  asiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ siddhaḥ sādhanañca iti unubhavāt  tadā sādhya tvam hi tadā sādhana tvasya virodhi niyamataḥ tena eva tasya pratikṣepeṇa saha anavasthāna niyamāt na tu sādhana tvasya anyadā sādhana tvasya vā tayoḥ apratikṣepāt  anyadā sādhana tve api sādhana tvam asti eva sāmānya abhāve viśeṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt  evantadā asiddhatvasya tadā siddha tvam virodhi niyamataḥ tasya eva pratikṣepāt  na tu siddhatva mātram anyat api tatra siddhatva abhāva prasaṅgāt  nirviśeṣitayoḥ virodhe ca siddha tvayoḥ ca anyataradeva pāka ādau syāt na tu samaya bhede api ubhayam na ca tadā kṛti sādhya tve sati tadā iṣṭa sādhanatva jñānam pravartakam ata eva vājapeyena yajeta iti atra yāgasya karaṇa avasthāyām siddha tvena na vājapeyasya sādhya tā ekadā tayoḥ virodhāt iti karma nāmadheya tvam na tu karaṇasya siddha tvena sādhyatva virodhaḥ yoga svarūpe tayoḥ sattvāt  atha viruddhayoḥ avacśebhedam ādaya ekatra pratītiḥ syāt  na ca kṛti sādhyatva iṣṭa sādhana tvayoḥ samaya bhedam ādaya ekatra pratītiḥ asti tathā liṅga abhāvāt iti ced  na sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhasya ukta tvāt evam siddhatva asiddha tvayoḥ bhāva abhāva rūpa tve api na virodhaḥ eka dharmi ga tvena māna siddha tvāt tasmāt  saṃyoga tadabhāvayoḥ iva yena prakāreṇa yayoḥ virodhaḥ tena tayoḥ eka dharmi gata tvam na pratīyate na tu rūpa antareṇa api iti api ca yadi sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ tadā tava api iṣṭa sādhana tvena kārya sādhana tvena vā kāryatvam na anumīyate hetu sādhyayoḥ virodhena sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāvena vyāpti asiddheḥ pakṣe sādhya sādhanayoḥ anyatara sattve bādhā asidhyoḥ anyatara prasaṅgāt ca na ca vācyam idānīm mad kṛti sādhya tvam sādhyam agre mad iṣṭa sādhana tvam hetuḥ daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati yad agre mad iṣṭa asā dhanam tad idānīm mad kṛti sādhyam iti vyāptiḥ tathā ca samaya bhedam ādāya sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ avagama iti idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt anugata rūpa abhāvena vyāpteḥ agrahāt  pāka nyāyena anyatra api tad tad samaya antarbhāvena sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ apratītiḥ pratītau vā mama api idānīm kṛti sādhya tve sati agre iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānam pravartakam astu na ca pāke sādhya iṣṭaka tvena kṛti sādhya tvam anumeyam asiddha avasthāvataḥ  hi pāka ādiṣṭa anutpatteḥ pākasya siddha tvam avagamya tad sādhya tvam iṣṭasya avagantavyam asiddha tvañcau  agamya kṛti sādhya tvam iti siddhatva asiddha tvayoḥ virodhaḥ  atra api durvāraḥ api ca sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janya kārya tā jñāna abhāvāt sukhe katham cikīrṣā na hi kṛti sādhya tā jñāna mātrāt sā sañjāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādau cikīrṣā prasaṅgāt  atha upāya cikīrṣāyām tad kāraṇam icchā karaṇa sukhatva jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam yadā viṣayaḥ tadā sukhe cikīrṣā naḥ ced icchā mātram iti dvayam eva cikīrṣā hetuḥ iti ced  tarhi icchā hetu jñāne yadā kṛti sādhya tvam bhāsate tāda cikīrṣā naḥ ced icchā mātram iti eva sukha tad upāya cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu lāghavāt  sukhatva jñānavat iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya api icchā kāraṇa tvāt ata eva pāke iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam viṣaya iti tatra cikīrṣā na tu vṛṣṭi ādi jñāne tad viṣaya tvam iti icchā mātram sukha cikīrṣāyām icchā kāraṇa jñāne kṛti sādhya tā viṣayake cikīrṣā janakatva avadhāraṇāt anyathā tatra cikīrṣā anutpatteḥ vastu tas tu upāya cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyā upāya icchā tvāt  vṛṣṭī icchāvat  na ca bhoga cikīrṣāvat tena vinā api sya āditi aprayoñjaka tvam upāya icchāyāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt vṛṣṭeḥ ca svatas  asundara tvena icchā anutpatteḥ anugata upāya icchāyām anugatasya prayojaka tve sambhavati bādhakam vinā tyāga ayogāt ca na ca cikīrṣā anya tve sati upāya it chā tvam icchā tvam vā tad janya tve prayojakam gauravāt  sukha icchāyām tad abhāvāt ca evañcopāya cikīrṣāyām iṣṭa sādhanatva jñāne dhruve ati prasaṅga vāraṇa artham kṛti sādhyatva nirvāha arthañca kṛti sādhya tvam api viṣaya tayā avacchedakam astu na tu tad vihāya tanmātram kḷpta kāraṇam vinā kārya anupapatteḥ ata eva stana pāna pravṛttau  api upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena gṛhītasya iṣṭa sādhanatva jñānasya api kalpanam dṛṣṭa anurodhi tvāt kalpanāyāḥ nanu sādhana tvam icchā virodhi tasya siddha dharma tvāt  vṛṣṭi ādau tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt iccha iti ced  na nirviśeṣitayoḥ siddhatva asiddha tvayoḥ avirodhena icchā sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhāt tadā asiddha tvam tadā siddhatvañca na icchā sādhana tvayoḥ prayojakam iti tathā na jñāyata eva yad tu tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt  vṛṣṭi ādau  icchā iti tad tuccham asiddha avasthāt vṛṣṭi ādeḥ iṣeṭa anutpatteḥ tasya avaśyam siddha tvam avagantavyam icchā anurodhi tvāt ca asiddha tvam iti tatra api virodha eva vṛṣṭau satyām iṣṭam tayā vinā na iti anvaya vyatireka grahasya vṛṣṭi siddha tvam ādāya vṛṣṭi nirūpita iṣṭa sādhyakatva grāhaka tvāt  kiñca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhyam maṇḍalīkaraṇam iti artha pratipādakam amaṇḍalīm kuryāt iti vākyam pramāṇam syāt viṣaya ābādhāt etena navīna matam api apāstam parasya hi kṛti sādhyatva odana kāma nāvattva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānānām jñānam tathā ātmana odana kāmān āvat tevaṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya jñānam na pravṛtti kāraṇam gauravāt  kintu mad kṛti sādhya tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva lāghavāt  yathā ca sādhyatva sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhaḥ anāgatasya pāka ādeḥ kṛti sādhyatva jñānañca tathā upapāditam eva kiñca para kṛti sādhya tvam ajñātvā api sva kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt  sva kalpita lipya ādau yauvane kāma udrekāt  sambhoga ādau pravṛtteḥ ca tad eva pravartakam vastutas tu siddha viṣaya ka kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt katham kṛtyā sādhayā ami iti icchā siddhe icchā virahāt asiddhasya ajñānāt  atha siddha viṣayāt eva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt asiddha viṣayā kṛti sādhya tvena icchā jñāyate icchāyā asiddha viṣayatva svabhāva tvāt eka prakāraka tvena jñāna cikīrṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  na tu eka viṣaya tve sati gauravāt  icchāyā anāgata viṣaya tvāt  tasya ca ajñānāt  tathātva darśanāt sukha ādi icchāyām api evam iti ced  na asiddha viṣaya icchā anu rodhena anāgata jñāna upāyasya darśita tvāt  astu ca evam tathā api kṛti sādhyatā jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva vyāvartaka m astu sva parakīya iṣṭa sā adhana tā jñāna phala kāmanā jñāna apekṣayā laghu tvāt  iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna jñānasya phala kāmanā jñānasya ca hetu tve māna abhāvāt ca navyāḥ tu sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam eva pravartakam tena sva kṛtya sādhye vṛṣṭi ādau kārīrya añca kṛṣīvalasya na pravṛttiḥ na ca sañjāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇe pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñāna viṣaye iṣṭa tvasya svarūpa satas  pravṛttau sahakāri tvāt  na ca sañjāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇāt ā  icchāsti iṣṭa sādhana tvena ajñānāt atīta bhojane api ata eva na pravartate tṛpteḥ siddha tayā icchā viraheṇa bhojane tad upādhika iṣṭatva abhāvāt atīta tṛptau  icchā na asti iti tad sādhane api iṣṭatva abhāvāt eva na pravṛttiḥ na ca evam pāke na pravarteta tasya svarasa taiṣṭatva abhāvāt iti vācyam iṣṭa sādhanatva jñānena tasya api iṣṭa tvāt hantā evam prāthamika tvāt iṣṭatva artham avaśya apekṣaṇīya tvāt ca kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu iti ced  na iṣṭa asādhanatva abhāve api bhoge cikīrṣā sattvāt tasyām sva kṛti sādhanatva abhāve api bhoge cikīrṣā sattvāt tasyām sva kṛti sādhyatva jñāne sati iṣṭa tvam eva kāraṇam na tu iṣṭa sādhana tvam vyabhicārāt  pāka ādau tad anvaya vyatirekau  apīṣṭatva upakṣāṇau evam bhoge api pravarteta iti ced  na iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api mukti rūpa iṣṭa sādhane sukhe pravarteta iti tulyam sukhe cikīrṣā bhavati eva kṛtiḥ tu na bhavati kṛteḥ siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣayatva niyamāt iti ced tulyam tasmāt  sva kṛti sādhya tvam vidhiḥ iṣṭa tvam sahakārī iti mā evam iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya upāya icchāyām hetutva avadhāraṇāt tasyāḥ tad janyatva niyamāt i  chāyāḥ sva viṣaya icchā anutpādakatva niyamāt ca nanu siddhaudanaḥ kutas  pāke na pravartate odana mātrasya siddha tvena iṣṭatva abhāvāt ata eva atīta bhojana ādau na pravartate atīta tṛṣṇā ādau  icchā virahāt nanu sāmudraka vikhyāte bhāvi yauvana rojye bhoga sādhane sva kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhanatva jñānāt  kutaḥ na pravartate bhāvi rājyasya asiddha tvāt pravatteḥ siddha viṣayatva niyamāt  rājya upāya aparicayāt ca tad paricaye ca pravartata eva devatā ārādhana ādau  iti ced  na siddhe cikīrṣā viraheṇa yāga ādau  api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt  devatā ārādhana ādeḥ api asiddha tve na tatra api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca kiñca rājya upayāparicaye tatra mā pravarttiṣṭa sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāne rājye pravṛtti prasaṅge kim āyātam na hi kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāne api tad upāya jñānam tatra pravartakam gauravāt  bhinna viṣaya tvāt ca iti ced  mā evam yauvane hi yāvat  pravartata eva rājye bālye tu rājya upāyam akṛtvā mad kṛtya idānīm rājyam na siddhyati iti sva kṛti asādhyata ajñānāt eva na pravartate yathā taṇḍulam vinā pāke sva kṛti asādhyata ajñānāt rājya upāye tu sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte devatā ārādhana ādau pravartata eva ata eva vrīhi avaghātam akṛtvā puroḍāśaḥ tam akṛtvā yāgaḥ tam akṛtvā apavūrvam sādhayitum na śakyata iti kramaśas  avaghāta ādau pravartate na yugapad  siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣaya aviṣaya svabhāva tvāt pravṛtteḥ yāga anantarañca na apūrve pravartate kṛti antaram vinā eva yāga kṛtitaḥ tad sambhavāt iṣṭa sādhane ceṣṭā utpattinā āntarīyaka duḥkha ājanaka tvam viśeṣaṇam na tu tad jñāna abhāvaḥ kāraṇam kintu tad eva viṣaya tayā kāraṇa tāvacchedakam lāghavāt  tena madhu viṣa sampṛkta anna bhojane na pravṛttiḥ pareṇa api pravṛtti pūrvam liṅga viśeṣaṇa tvena anyathā vā tad jñāna viniyoga svīkārāt evañca alpa āyāsa sādhya ādiṣṭa utpatti sambhave bahu āyāsa sādhye na pravṛttiḥ ata eva śruta svarga phalaka tve api bahu vitta vyayāsa sādhye jyotiṣṭoma ādau phala bhūmā kalpane anyathā alpa āyāsa asadhyāt eva svarga siddhi sambhave tatra apravṛttau ananuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam aprāmāṇyam tad vidheḥ syāt  balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvañca na viśeṣaṇam bahu vitta vyaya āyāsa sādhya bahutara duḥkhasya api abalavat tvam kvacid alpa duḥkhasya api balavat tvam tasya api ukta atiriktasya ananugamāt  āstikasya niṣiddha tvena jñāte api pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena naraka sādhanatva jñāna tirodhānāt nanu na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti atra vidhi artha niṣedha anupapattiḥ tad bhakṣaṇasya tṛpti rūpa iṣṭa sādhana tvāt  na ca asura avidyā ādivat  paryudāsa lakṣaṇayā virodhi aniṣṭa sādhanatva bodhanam nañaḥ  asamasta tvāt  kriyā saṅgata tvena pratiṣadha vācakatva vyutpatteḥ ca iti ced  na viśeṣyavati viśiṣṭa niṣedhasya sa viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena viśeṣaṇa niṣedha paryavamāyitayā kalañja bhakṣaṇam iṣṭa utpattinā antarīyaka duḥkha atirikta duḥkha sādhanam iti na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti anena bodhanāt  iṣṭa sādhana tā vācakasya siddheḥ sāmānyatas  niṣedha anupapatteḥ balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhanatva viśeṣa niṣedha tātparyam tathā ca aśakya viśeṣa niṣedha para tvam naña iti kaścid  tad na yathā hi ayogya tayā sa  chidram vihāya ghaṭa tvena tad itara anvayaḥ  na tu chidretara tvena yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhāt tathā atra api balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhi tvena anupasthitau katham tad niṣedhaḥ śyenena abhicaran yajeta iti atra katham vidhi pravṛttiḥ hiṃsāyāḥ  balavat aniṣṭa anubandhi tvāt iti ced  tatra kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhantvam eva yogyatayā anveti na tu balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhi tvam api ayogya tvāt  nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca hiṃsāyāḥ  balavat aniṣṭa anubandhitva avagamāt  ata eva vihite apiśyene vigānāt na tātvika pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena aniṣṭa anubandhi aṃśasya tiraskārāt  kasyacid  pravṛttiḥ iti eke anye tu abhicārasya vairi badha phalaka tvena śruta tvāt  badha sādhana tvena śyenaḥ  vidhīyate na tu badha sādhya naraka sādhana tvena narakasya phala tvena aśruteḥ na ca janaka janakasya janakatva niyamaḥ kumbhakāra pitṛ paramparāyāḥ kumbha janakatva āpatteḥ vidhinā eva śyenasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhitva bodhanāt ca na ca śyenasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhitva bodhanāt ca na ca śyenasya naraka ahetu tve apekṣita vairi badha hetu tve vā avigānena pravṛttiḥ syāt iti vācyam śyenāt badhaḥ badhāt ca avaśyam naraka iti pratisandhānena vigānāt  nanu śyenaḥ maraṇa phalaka vyāpāra tvena hiṃsā sā ca naraka janikā iti ced  na na hi sākṣāt  paramparā sā dhāraṇa maraṇa phala kavyāpāraḥ  hiṃsā kūpa ādau vinaṣṭe gavi tad karttuḥ gobadha kaṛttutva āpatteḥ badhyasya api hantuḥ mṛtyu utpādana dvāreṇa ātma hantṛtva prasaṅgāt ca na hi anutpādita manyuḥ kaścid  kam api vyāpādayati kintu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phala kovyā pāraḥ  hiṃsā yad anantaram maraṇam bhavati eva na ca śyenaḥ tathā kintu khaṅga hanana ādikam eva atha maraṇān uddeśena kṣipta nārācāt hata brāhyaṇe ca hiṃsā na syāt  kiñca hinasti dhātu arthe avacchedakam phalam avyavahitam eva maraṇam avyavahita phalakasya eva vyāpārasya dhātu vācya tvāt  anyathā paramparayā vilkipti phalaka anna kāma iṣṭa taṇḍula kraya ādau  api pacati iti prasaṅgāt  evam khaṅga abhighāta anantaram yatra vilambena maraṇam vraṇa pāka paramparayā vā anne viṣa prayogeṇa vā tatra hantṛ tvam prāyaścitta ādi ca na syāt  iti ced  na prāyaścitta tulya tā artham hi tatra hantṛvyadeśaḥ  gauṇaḥ vinigama kañca lāghavam eva vastutas tu maraṇa uddeśena kṛtaḥ  adṛṣṭādvārākaḥ tad anukūla vyāpāraḥ  hiṃsā kūpa ādau vinaṣṭe gavi tad kartuḥ gaḥ badhaka ṛtutva āpatteḥ badhyasya api hantuḥ mutyu utpādana dvāreṇa ātma hantṛtva prasaṅgāt ca na hi anutpādita manyuḥ kaścid  kam api vyāpādayati kintu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phala kovyā paraḥ  hiṃsā yad anantaram maraṇam bhavati eva na ca śyenaḥ tathā kintu khaṅga hanana ādikam eva atha maraṇa ānukūlī vyāpāraḥ  maraṇa uddaśena anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ  hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca tathā kūpa ādau ca na maraṇa uddeśena anuṣṭhīyamāna tvam iti ced  na evam sati gauravāt  maraṇān uddeśena kṣipta nārācāt hata brāhmaṇe ca hiṃsā na syāt  kiñca hinasti dhātu arthe avacchedakam phalam avyavahitam eva maraṇam avyavahita phalakasya eva vyāpārasya dhātu vācya tvāt  anyathā paramparayā viklitti phalaka anna kāma iṣṭa taṇḍula kraya ādau  api pacati iti prasaṅgāt  evam khaṅga abhighāta anantaram yatra vilambena maraṇam vraṇa pāka paramparayā vā anne viṣa prayogeṇa vā tatra hantṛ tvam prāyaścitta ādi ca na syāt  iti ced  prāyaścitta tulya tā artham hi tatra hantṛ vyapadeśaḥ  gauṇaḥ vinigama kañca lāghavam eva vastutas tu maraṇa uddeśena kṛtaḥ  adṛṣṭāt vārakaḥ tad anukūlī vyāpāraḥ  hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvāra kastanukūlya vyāpāraḥ  hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvārā maraṇa sādhanam atas  na hiṃsā yadi ca adṛṣṭa dvārā api maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā syāt  tadā saptamī taila abhyaṅgasya adṛṣṭa dvārā iṣṭa bhārya vināśa hetu tvāt abhyaṅga kartu hiṃsakatva āpattiḥ ata eva kūpa ādau gomaraṇe api na badha kartu tvam tad kartuḥ gala lagna anna maraṇe na bhoktuḥ na vā pariveṣayituḥ ātma hantṛ tvam brahma hantṛ tvam vā vraṇa pāka paramparayā vilambena viṣa prayogeṇa ca hantṛ tvam mukhyam eva na tu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phalaka tvam gala lagna anna maraṇe sva hantṛtva āpatteḥ anya uddaśena kṣipta nārācena hate brāhmaṇe brahma hantṛ tvam syāt iti ced  na iṣṭa āpatteḥ vyapadeśaḥ tu gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ lakṣaṇayā api samarthayitum śakyate tad pakṣe ati prasaṅgaḥ vārayitum na śakyata iti idam eva vinigamakam ata eva atad uddeśena kṛte api niṣiddhe prāyaścitta arddham uktam apare tu anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā khaṅga kārasya anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāra dvārā maraṇa sādhana tvam tasya hi nara antara vyāpāra dvārā maraṇa sādhana tvam tasya hi nara antara vyāpāraḥ  nābhisaṃhitaḥ kintu dhana lābha iti khaṅga kāraḥ  na ghātakaḥ viṣasya anne prakṣepeṇa nara antara vyāpāraḥ  bhojanam eva abhisaṃhitaḥ anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya viṣa prayogāt iti hisā eva anne viṣa prayoga iti tad na gala lagna kavalāt yatra maraṇam tatra pariveṣayituḥ ghātaka tā āpātāt  anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya parivaṣaṇāt bhoktuḥ ātma hantṛtva āpatteḥ ca anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa anukūlānnaṃbhakṣaṇa anuṣṭhānāt ata eva avyavahita prāṇa viyoga phala kaḥ  vyāpāraḥ  hiṃsā vraṇa pāka paramparā mṛte tu hantṛ tvam vyāpārasya avyavadhāyaka tvāt iti nirastam syāt etad  na iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhiḥ nitye sandhyā upāsana ādau phala abhāvāt atha na asti eva tad  nityam yatra artha vāda ādikam vidhi vākye vā na phalam śrutam asti sandhyām upāsate ye tu satatam śaṃsita vratāḥ vidhūta pāpāḥ te yānti brahma lokam sanātanam iti ādi artha vādāt  dadyāt aharahar  śrāddham pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āvahan ityādi vidhi vākya śravaṇāt ca kṛtvā acintayātu ucyate yatra na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajinnayāyāt  svargaḥ phalam iti ced  na kāmanā upādhi kārya tvena yāgavat nitya tā bhaṅga prasaṅgāt aharahar  śrutyā hi tad kāla jīvi mātra kṛti sādhyam sandhyā vandanam avagatam hi kāmanā upādhi kārya tve ca yadā phala kāmanā na asti tadā tad samaya eva tad kartavyatā na syāt  na hi tad kāle phala kāmanā vaśyambhāvaḥ pramāṇa bhāvāt  kiñca prathama pravṛtta itara nirapekṣā harahar  śrutyā jīvi mātrasya adhikāraḥ  avagataḥ tathā ca tad sa apekṣa caram apravṛtti artha vāda upanīta phala kāmasya na tatra adhikāraḥ prathama pravṛttā aharahar śruti virodhāt nitye phala śruteḥ artha vādasya ca stutau tātparyam ata eva pratyavāya parihāraḥ  api na phalam tad kāmanā upādhi kārya tve nitya tā kṣateḥ kiñca nitye kartavya tā bodhanāt prāk  na pratyavāye pramāṇam asti vidheḥ kartavya tvam avagamya kartavyā karaṇe pratyavāya kalpanam yena anyonya āśrayaḥ kintu nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca upāsanasya prakṛti arthasya tāvat vyāpāra svarūpasya abhāvaḥ pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ tathā ca sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ pratyavāya dvārā duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ sandhyā upāsanam duḥkha sādhana abhava tvena phalam prāyaścitte pāpa dhvaṃsavat iti tad sādhana tvena kṛtiḥ bodhyate vidhinā na ca evam pratyavāya parihāra eva phalam astu iti vācyam parihārasya prāc abhāva rūpa tvena anāditayā asādhya tvāt  na ca upāsana ākaraṇam pratyavāya hetuḥ na upāsana abhāvaḥ tathā ca duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena kṛtiḥ iṣṭā na tu upāsanam iti vācyam nindā artha vādasya ubhayatra sattvena ubhayasya api tathā tvāt iti tad na evam api kāmya tve nitya tā kṣati prasaṅgāt  kiñca akurvan vihitam karma ityādinā na upāste yaḥ ca paścimām ityādinā ca karaṇa abhāvasya eva pratyavāya hetu tvam bodhyate na tu tad viṣaya abhāvasya anyathā akartuḥ pratyavāyaḥ  na anyasya iti katham syāt  viṣaya abhāvasya sādharaṇyāt  vastutas tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam pravartaka tvena nirvyūḍham na ca kṛtau kṛti sādhya tvam asti iti atas  na kiñcid etad  navyāḥ tu nitya apūrva prāgabhāvaḥ  durita dvārā duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ  apūrvam duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena iṣṭam tad sādhana tvena kṛti sādhya tvena ca sandhyā upāsanam vidhīyate iti tad na nindā artha vāda ādinā sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ tad akaraṇam vā pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ  na tu apūrvā bhāvaḥ prathamam pramāṇa abhāvena tad anupasthiteḥ vidheḥ iṣṭa sādhanatva bodhaka tvāt  pariśeṣeṇa apūrvam iṣṭam kalpyata iti ced  tarhi viśvajinnayāyena svarga eva phalam kalpyatām kāmya tvasya tvayā api svīkārāt  kiñca vidhi pravṛttau  apūrva jñānam apūrva jñāne ca vidhi pravṛttiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ yāvat nitya naimittika nirvāhasya tad tad āśrayam avihita karmaṇām samyak paripālanasya ca brahma loka avāptiḥ phalam śrūyate tathā ca nityasya saphala tvam iti kecid  tad na tasya vidheḥ nitya vidhim upajīvya pravṛttiḥ tasya ca phala abhāvena prathamam mūka tvāt  anyathā paraspara sāpekṣa tvena anyonya āśrayaḥ tasmāt  kārya tā eva vidhiḥ nanu nitye vedāt  kārya tā jñāne api prayojana jñānam vinā katham pravṛttiḥ na hi prayojanam uddiśya mandaḥ api pravartate iti ced  na nitye phala bādhena pravṛtti mātre prayojana jñānasya aprayojaka tvāt  kāmye api prayojana jñānam na sākṣāt  pravartakam upāya viṣaya tvāt  prayojane apravṛtteḥ ca kintu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna dvārā kārya tā jñāne upakṣīṇam eva katham ayam niścayaḥ nitye iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna asambhavāt kārya tā ajñānasya vedāt api sambhavāt  nanu niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā prekṣāvatām katham pravṛttiḥ veda adhīna kārya tā jñāna sattvāt saphala pravṛttau  api tasya eva tantra tvāt yad tu laukike niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā na pravartate tad iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakasya kārya tā ajñānasya veda adhīnasya vā abhāvāt  na ca duḥkha eka phalatva jñānam pravṛtti pratibandhakam sati kārya tā jñāne tasya pratibandhakatva adarśanāt  atha vā kāmye liṅgaḥ  apūrva vācatvāt nitye api liṅga upāsana ādi viṣaya kamapūrvam bodhyate tad ca niṣphalam api stata eva sukhavat prayojanam nityam abhyarthyam ānañca iti ucyate sarvatra nitye phala śravaṇa jīvi phala kāmasya sambalita adhikāraḥ yathā uparāge naimittikam snāna śrāddha ādi phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe prāyaścitta ādi śruteḥ ca niyata kartavya tākam yathā vā ṣoḍaśa śrāddhasya pretatva vimukti kāmanā śruteḥ pretatva vimukti hetu ṣoḍaśa śrāddhe saṅkalpam vidhāya mahājanānām ācārāt kāmya tvam nindā artha vādena akaraṇe pratyavāya śruteḥ vaśya kartavya tvam tathā sandhyā upāsanam api phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca niyata kartavya tāka tvam tad akaraṇe prāyaścitta anupadeśāt na ca nitye phala kāmanāyā asambhavaḥ tri kāla kamyaḥ tava pāṭhavat  nitye phala kāmanā sambhavāt yad tu prathama pravṛttā aharahar śrutyā tad kāla jīvi mātrasya adhikāra bodhanāt na phala kāmasya adhikāra iti tad na aharahar śruti artha vādayoḥ prathama gṛhīta eka vākyatā balena tad kāla jīvi phala anvayam vinā eka vākyata aṅgāt na ca artha vādasya stuti paratva at na eka vākyatā bādhakam vinā sva artha parityāgāt  vidhivā vākya upasthite phale vidhi vākya stha phalam ādāya eva aharahar śrutyā kārya tā bodhanāt nanu evam tad kāla jīvikām inaḥ  adhikāre yadā phala kāmanā virahaḥ tadā aśuceḥ iva adhikāra abhāvāt niyata kartavyatā na syāt  adhikṛta akaraṇe pratyavāyaḥ  na tu akaraṇa mātra iti ced  na naimittike api tad kāle kasyacid kāmanā virahiṇaḥ  aniyata kartavyatā āpatteḥ atha apavāda abhāvena otsikī phala kāmanā asti eva phala jñānasya sva viṣaya ka icchā janaka svabhāvāt yasya tu mumukṣa apavādena phala antare kāmanā na asti tasya akaraṇe api na pratyavāya iti na tad niyata kartavya tāka tvam naimittike tathā nitye api mumukṣayā phala kāmanā bādhena akaraṇe api na pratyavāya iti tulyam kiñca arthavāda upasthita phala upādhi kartavya tve avagate akurvan vihitam karma ityādi vākyāt śauce sati sandhyau  andhākaraṇe nindā artha vādena ca naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca pratyavāyaḥ kalpyate tad phala kāmanā virahe api pratyavāya parihāra artham niyamataḥ pravartate vidhi pravṛtti anantaram pratyavāyasya prāmāṇika tvāt  akaraṇa unmukhasya karaṇena pratyavāya pragābhāvasya sādhya tvāt  naimittike phala upādhi kartavya tve kāmanā virahe api niyata kartavya tāvat  yad tu niṣphale api nitye veda ādīn akārya tā ajñānāt pravartata iti tad na duḥkha eka phala tvena jñāyamāne prekṣāvatām kṛteḥ anutpāda niyamāt  ayogya tayā nitye kṛti sādhya tvasya bodhayitum aśakyatvāt  ata eva sandhyā upāsana phalam api kriyate veda bodhita kartavya tāka tvāt iti āśaṅkya guru matam etad na guroḥ matam iti abhiprāyeṇa upekṣitavān ācāryaḥ yad tu pāṇḍa apu urvam svata eva prayojanam iti uktam tad api na evam tava api kāmya tve nityatva hāni āpatteḥ kiñca sukham duḥkha abhāvaḥ ca mukhyam prayojanam tad sādhanañca gauṇam nitya āpūrvantu prayojanam pravartaka vidhi anurodhena tad api pravartakam kalpyata iti ced  na pravartanīyena lokena tasya prayojana tvena ajñānāt guruṇā nitya apūrvam prayojana m uktam iti ucyamāne api na ādaraḥ prekṣāvatām mukti svargau cālaukikau  api sukha duḥkha abhāvasa jātīya tayā prayojane tasmāt evam vadan guruḥ api laghuḥ eva tad ayam saṅkṣepaḥ nitye duḥkha eka phala tvena pravṛtti anupapatteḥ phala upādhi kartavya tā tad ca phalam duḥkha sādhana abhāvaḥ pāṇḍa apu urvam vā iti tad icchā pravṛtti artham pratyaham upeyā tām vinā pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tathā ca artha vādikam vidhi vākya śru tañca phalam astu kṛtam anyena na ca kāmanā virahe niyata kartavyatā na syāt  apūrva ādi icchā virahe api tulya tvāt  pratyavāya parihāra artham niyamataḥ pravṛttiḥ tulyā eva yatra ca na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajit nayāya iti nanu idam iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt etad sādhyam iṣṭam iti jñānāt ca pravṛtti darśanāt  prathamasya eva pravartaka tve kim vinigamakam ucyate phala icchāyām sva viṣaya viśeṣya ka jñānasya hetu tvena kḷpta tvāt  upāya cikīrṣā api bādhakam vinā tathā vastutas tu kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhya iṣṭa iti jñānasya pravartaka tve yajeta iti padāt  prathamam kṛti sādhyaḥ  yāga iti jñānam tatas  kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhya iṣṭa iti jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna sādhya tvāt viśiṣṭa jñānasya iti jñāna dvayam tava mama tu yāgaḥ kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhanam iti ekam eva jñānam na ca kṛti sādhya tvam yāge bodhayitvā kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhya iṣṭa iti liṅgā bodhayitum śakyam api eka sva artha anvayam apara padārthe bodhayitvā tad anvita apara sva artha anvaya bodhaka tvasya pade avyuptatteḥ yajipade ca kṛtyā saha yāga anvayam bodhayitvā tad anvita apara sva artha anvaya bodhaka tvasya pade avyutpatteḥ yajipade ca kṛtyā saha yāga anvayam bodhayitvā paryavasite punar  sva artha anvaya bodhaka tve āvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ atha sādhyam iṣṭam yasya iti sādhya iṣṭaka tvam śakyam tathā ca bahuvrrīhi artha apekṣayā iṣṭasya sādhanam iti padi arthasya laghu tvāt tad eva śakyam kiñca tad sādhya tvam na niyamataḥ tad uttara sattvam daṇḍa sādhye ghaṭe vyabhicārāt  na api tad avacchinna kṣaṇa uttarakṣaṇa eva sattvam eva kāra vyavacchedya tad anuttara samayasya ākāśe aprasiddheḥ śabdasya tad asādhyatva āpatteḥ ata eva na tad abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyāgi tvam rūpe rasa sādhyatva āpatteḥ ca na api tad avadhika uttaratva vyāpya samaya sambandhaḥ uttaratva vyāpya tvam hi uttaratva anadhikaraṇa kāla āvṛtti tvam tad ca ākāśe aprasiddham gurutarañca tasmāt  tad sādhanaka tvam eva tad sādhya tvam evañca lāghavāt  tad sādhanatva jñānam eva pravartakam na tu tad sādhanakatva jñānam iti syāt etad  iṣṭatva jñānasya pravartaka tve tṛptaḥ  api bhojane pravarteta manasā tṛpteḥ iṣṭatva jñānāt atha svarūpasatī api phala icchā kāraṇam sā ca siddha tayā tṛptau na asti iti ced  tarhi hantā evam āvaśyaka tvāt  phala icśā eva kāraṇam na tu tad jñānam gauravāt  kiñca icchā jñānasya kāraṇa tve icchā kāraṇam na syāt  sva jñānena tad nāśāt icchā tad jñāna dhārā kalpane anavasthānāt  api ca icchā viṣayaḥ sukham iti jñānam na mānasam sukhasya asiddha tayā tad viśeṣyaka sākṣātkārasya tad sannikarṣam vinā abhāvāt  odana ādau  api iṣṭatva jñānam na sambhavati manāsaḥ bahirasvātantrāt na api cakṣuḥ ādinā jñātaḥ kṛta itivat  iṣṭatva jñānam tatra viśeṣya sannikarṣāt  vastutas tu iṣṭasya viśiṣya sukhatva ādinā ajñāne yāga pākādāviṣṭa sādhana tā jñānepya pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iṣṭasya apalpa adhika bhāvena nānā prakāra tvena ca viśiṣya anadhyavasāyāt  na ceṣṭa viṣaya tā avacchedaka sukhatva ādeḥ upalakṣaṇam iṣṭa tvam sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhaneṣu anugatasya upalakṣyasya abhāvena ananugamāt iti ucyate yatra icchā tad sādhana tā jñānam eva loka vedasā dhāraṇam pravartakam teṣām sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana tvena icchā viṣayāṇām ananugatānām api vastu sadicchā viṣaya tvam eva anugamakam evam yadā sukha ādau  icchā bhavati sva kṛti sādhya tve sati sukha ādi sādhanam iti jñānam tadā pāka ādau pravartate nanu evam pravartaka jñāna viṣasya nānā tvena tad śaktasya vidhi pratyayasya nānā arthatva prasaṅga iti ced  na sukhatva ādinā ananugatam iṣṭa tvena anugatam phalam prati sādhana tvasya yāga ādeḥ liṅga ādinā bodhanāt  tathā ca phalānām anugama artham phala icchā śakyā na tu icchā jñāna kāraṇa tvena atha evam sukha ādi sādhana tvena jñānam pravartakam tad na śakyam ananugamāt  yad ca śakyam iṣṭa sādhana tvam tad jñānam na pravartakam iti vidheḥ pravartaka tā na syāt  iti ced  sākṣāt evam eva kintu iṣṭa sādhanam yāga eti liṅgā bodhite iṣṭa ākāṅkṣāyām kāmya tvena śrutaḥ svarga eva iṣṭa tvena avagamyate tad anantaram svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāt svarga sādhanam yāga iti jñānam pravartakam utpadyate evañca vidhi janya jñāna janyam jñānam pravartakam yad tu sarveṣām eva vidheḥ na sākṣāt  pravartakam vidhi bodhakāt  sva kṛti sādhyatva ādeḥ anavagamāt  sva iṣṭa sādhanatvañca aham iṣṭa sādhana yāgakaḥ svarga kāma tvāt darśa vākya avagata svarga kāmavat iti anantaram arthāt  pratīyate tad na yatra icchā tad sādhanam iti śābda jñānāt eva pravṛtti upapatteḥ tad pratītiḥ niṣphalā anye tu sādhanatva mātram vidhi arthaḥ svarga ādi sādhana tālā bhaḥ tu samabhivyāhārāt  iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tasya upajīvya tvāt tathā hi yajeta iti anena yāgaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ sādhanañca iti bodhite sādhanasya sādhya akāṅkṣāyām kāmanā viṣaya tvena śrutī asiddhaḥ svarga eva sādhana ākāṅkṣaḥ  sādhya tvena avagamyate upasthita tvāt  na ca yāgasya sādhana ākāṅkṣā kṛti sādhya tvena eva upasthiteḥ ata eva viśva jit ādau svarga eva sādhya tvena kalpyata iti iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe api tarati mṛtyum tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ  aśvamedhena yajate iti ādi artha vāde vidhi kalpanam iti ced  na avinā abhāvāt  tathābhūta sādhana tvasya vidheyatva vyāpta tvāt  vyāpaka anupalambha bādha udadvārāya vā prayojana abhāvāt na tad kalpanam tatra iti api āhuḥ yad tu iṣṭa sādhanatva abhidhāne karaṇe liṅgaḥ  anuśāsanāt  darśa paurṇamāsābhyām iti anabhihita adhikāra vihitā tṛtīyā na syāt iti tad na upāya tā mātra abhidhāne api tad viśeṣa karaṇatva anabhidhānāt vastutastu abhihita anvaya labhyam yāga iṣṭa sādhana tvam iṣṭa sādhanatva mātrasya vidhi artha tvāt  navyāḥ tu cikīrṣā dvārā jñānasya kṛtau hetu tā cikīrṣā ca kṛtau  icchā sanaḥ prakṛti artha gocara icchā vāci tvāt pipakṣa ādivat  na tu kṛti viṣaya pāka ādi viṣaye kṛti sādhyatva prakāraka icchā abhidhāyaka tvam pāka ādeḥ prakṛti anabhidheya tvāt  na hi kṛti vācakasya tad viṣaya vācaka tvam karoti iti ukte tad viṣaya saṃśayāt evañca kṛta āviccheṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vā vṛṣṭi ādau tathā kalpanāt  yadā ca kṛtau  icchā tadā sā eva cikīrṣā anyatra icchā mātram na tu kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt kṛtau kṛti sādhyatva abhāvāt atha pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā anubhava siddhā anubhava apalāpe upekṣaṇīyatva āpatteḥ sā ca kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt sā ca cikīrṣā pada apratipādya api kṛti hetuḥ samāna viṣaya tvāt  na tu kṛti icchā kṛti hetuḥ kṛti viṣaya aviṣaya tvāt iti ced  asti tāvat pāka kṛtau  icchā vṛṣṭī icchāvat  asti ca kṛti sādhyatva prakārikā icchā pāke tathā api kṛti icchā eva kṛti kāraṇam lāghavāt  na tu kṛti sādhyatva prakārikā icchā gauravāt  dhātu arthān uparakte kṛti svarūpe icchā eva na udeti iti ced  na pāka ādi kṛti iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt pāka kṛtau  icchā tatas  kṛtiḥ iti abhyupagamāt  na ca avagati pravṛttyoḥ samāna viṣaya tvam ubhaya siddham tasya eva vicārya tvāt  katham tarhi pākam kṛtyā sādhayā ami iti icchā yathā vahni sādhya tvena iṣṭa sādhana tā avagamāt vahninā pākam sādhayā ami iti icchā tathā kṛti sādhya tvena iṣṭa sādhana tvāt  pākasya pākam kṛtyā sādhayā ami iti icchā anyathā tad tad upāya sādhya tvena icchā pāka ādau tad tad upāya sādhyatva prakāraka jñānāt syāt iti ananta kāraṇa kalpanā syāt  mama tu upāya icchāyām iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva hetuḥ kriyā dvārā kṛteḥ iṣṭa sādhanatva jñāne kriyāyāḥ  api iṣṭa sādhana tvam viṣaya eti kṛti icchā bhavantī kriyā viṣayā api bhavati iti jñāna icchā prayatnānām samāna viṣaya tā api ata eva pākam cikīrṣati iti cikīrṣā viṣaya tayā pākaḥ pratīyate yad vā icchā viṣaya viṣaya tayā pākaḥ pratīyate ita tasya karma tā grāmam jigamiṣati śatrum jighāṃsati iti atra grāma ādeḥ iva na hi grāma ādau  icchā siddha tvāt  ata eva bhoge sukhe ca cikīrṣā tad anukula kṛteḥ iṣṭa hetu tvāt anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe tad cikīrṣā sāmagṣantaram kalpyate evañca sandhyā vandanam duḥkha sādhana avandana abhāva rūpa tvena iṣṭam tad sādhanam kṛtiḥ iti liṅgarthaḥ anyathā kṛtiḥ na kṛti sādhyā sandhyā vandanañca na iṣṭa sādhanam iti kasya kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam vidhi arthaḥ syāt  ata eva eka pratyaya abhidheyatva pratyāsatteḥ antaraṅga tayā vidhi pratyaya abhidheya iṣṭa sādhana tvasya kṛtau  eva anvayaḥ  na prakṛti arthe tathā eva cikīrṣā kāraṇa jñāna janaka tvāt  prakṛti arthasya ca kṛtau viṣaya tvena anvaya iti ucyate vahni sādhya tvena kṛti sādhya tvena vā na pākasya odana sādhana tā iti uktam katham tarhi vahninā pākam sādhayā ami iti icchā iti ced  na iṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte yatra yad sādhya tvam jñāyate tatra tad sādhya tvena icchā bhavati iti yatheṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte pāke vahni sādhya tvena avagate iṣṭasya sādhana tā jñānāt kṛtyā sādhayā ami iti icchā tathā ceṣṭā sādhana tvena kṛti sādhya tvena ca jñāte kṛti sādhyatva prakārikā icchā na tu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna mātrāt iti acāryāḥ tu pravartakam iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva liṅga ṛtaḥ tu āptabhiprāyaḥ  lāghavāt  pākam kuryāḥ kuryām iti atra vidhi liṅgaḥ sambodhya sva kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhāyaka tvena jñā prārthanā śaṃsana ādi liṅgaḥ  vaktra ādi icchā abhidhāyaka tvena liṅga mātrasya icchā vācakatva kalpanāt ca evañca svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti asya svarga kāmasya kṛti sādhya tayā yāgaḥ  yāga yatnaḥ  vā āpteṣṭa iti arthaḥ tatas  yaḥ  vyāpāraḥ yasya kṛti sādhya tayā yad vyāpāra viṣayakaḥ prayatnaḥ  vā yasya āptena iṣyate sa tasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhanam iti vyāpti grahāt  yāgasya iṣṭa sādhana tvam anuminoti tathā hi yāgaḥ  mad iṣṭa sādhanam mad prayatna viṣaya tayā āptena iṣyamāṇa tvāt  yathā mad pitrā mad prayatna viṣayatayeṣyamāṇam mad bhojanam mad iṣṭa sādhanam tathā ca idam tasmāt tathā evam na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti asya mama kalañja bhākṣa prayatnaḥ  na āpta it chā viṣaya iti arthaḥ tatas  kalañja bhakṣaṇam mama balavat aniṣṭa sādhanam mad iṣṭa sādhana tve sati api āptena mad prayatna viṣaya tayā aniṣyamāṇa tvāt  yathā mad pitrā mad prayatna viṣaya tayā aniṣyamāṇaṇam madhu viṣa sampṛkta anna bhojanam mama balavat aniṣṭa sādhanam tathā ca idam tasmāt tathā sa ca āptaḥ  veda vyākhyātā bhagavān īśvara eva yaḥ tu vede pauruṣeya tvam na upaiti tam prati vidhiḥ eva tau  aṅgarbha iva śruti kumāryāḥ puṃyoge pramāṇam na tarhi lāghavam tātparya gauravāt i īśvara ādi ananta kalpanāt iti ced  na lāghava ādinā icchā bodhaka tvena loke liṅgaḥ pramāṇa siddha tvena phala mukha gauravasya adoṣa tvāt na tu kartuḥ asmaraṇam bādhakam prāk eva nirāsāt  tṛptikām anayā viṣa bhakṣaṇa pravṛttasya viṣa bhakṣaṇam tad  kṛti sādhya tayā na īśvareṇa iṣyate tatas  viṣa bhakṣaṇasya īśvara icchā viṣaya tve api na tena vyabhicāraḥ yad vā ratkāma kṛti sādhya tvena yaḥ  vyāpāra āptena iṣyate sa tasya iṣṭa sādhanam viṣa bhakṣaṇañca tṛpti kāma kṛti sādhya tvena na īśvara icchā viṣayaḥ māna abhāvāt ata eva na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti atra kalañja bhakṣaṇam tṛptikām anayā bhakṣaṇa pravṛttasya kṛti sādhya tvena āpta icchā viṣayaḥ  na iti tasya īśvara icchā viṣaya tve api viśiṣṭa niṣedha upapadyate abhiprāya vidhi pakṣe balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhitva mānu mānikam iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe tu tad api śakyam iti gauravam iti apūrvavāda pūrva pakṣaḥ atha svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti ādau  iṣṭa sādhana tvam kāryatvam vā yad vidhiḥ sa samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvayī tad anyā anvayī vā atra guravaḥ na ahatya kriyā kārya tayā liṅgā bodhayitum śakyate svarga kāma niyojya anvaya yogya tā jñāna virahāt kāmanā viśiṣṭasya hi mama idam kāryam iti boddhṛ tvam niyojya tvam tad  kāmanāyāḥ tad bodha upayoge sati bhavati sa ca kāmanā anantaram kāmya sādhana tā bodhanāt kārya tā bodhe sati syāt  evañca svarga sādhana tā bodhe sati svarga kāma niyojya anvaya yogya tā na ca kāla antara bhāvi svarge kriyā sākṣāt  paramparayā vā sādhanam iti śabdaḥ  bodhayitum arhati āśu vināśi tvāt  paramparā ghaṭakān upasthiteḥ ca tṛtīya prakāra abhāvāt ca anyathā tam ādāya sādhanatva sambhavāt  kalpyam api apūrvam na syāt  iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe sphuṭā eva anupapattiḥ kārya tā vidhi pakṣe anvaya prakāra tayā sādhana tvam śābdam iti phalataḥ na kaścid viśeṣaḥ atas  kriyātaḥ anyat  svarga sādhana tā arham kriyā kārya tā nirvāhakam liṅga ādi arthaḥ nanu sva jātīye anvaya darśanam yogya tā dṛṣṭañca ghṛta pānasya āśu vināśinaḥ kāla antare puṣṭi hetu tvam iti ced  na yathā kathañcit sājātyasya ayogye api sattvena yogyatayā avyāvartakatva āpatteḥ padārtha tāvacchedakena sājātyasya ādya jātaḥ payaḥ pibati ityādau prakṛte ca asambhavāt tasmāt anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvam sājātyam ata eva drava dravya tvam seka karaṇa tve prayojakam iti ayogyaḥ vahniḥ tad iha āśu vināśinaḥ kāla antara bhāvi phala janaka tve phala samaya paryanta sthāyi vyāpāra janaka tvam prayojaka matas  apūrvam vinā sājātyam eva na gṛhyate ghṛta pānasya tu vaidya ka upasthita dhātu sāmyam ādāya puṣṭi sādhanatva yogya tā jñānam vijñasya atha bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ  yogya tā na ca sādhanatva mātre bādhakam sākṣāt dbodhe api paramparā sādhana tvam ādāya tad viśrānti sambhavāt na ca yogyā anupalabdhā dvārasya bādhāt  paramparā sādhana tvam api bādhitam saṃskāsya iva tasya sambhavāt  anyathā vācye api apūrve kriyā kāmi kāryā na syāt  kāmya asādha tvāt na hi yad eva ayogyam tad paścāt  yogyam ayogya tve ca niṣphalaḥ prayāsaḥ na ca kāmi kāryam apūrvam tad arthi kāryā ca kriyā iti vācyam yāge rāgāt iti anena virodhāt  tathā api dvāra anupasthityā paramparā sādhanam iti jñānam na bhavet iti ced  satyam kintu svarga sādhanam yāga iti jñānam sākṣāt parampara uda āsīnam vastu gatyā paramparā sādhanatva viṣayakam utpadyamānam na ayogya tayā paribhavitum śakyam yadi ca sākṣāt paramparā viśeṣa dvaya vyatiriktam sāmānyam na asti eva tadā ananugamaḥ kim vā viśeṣayasi sākṣāt paramparayā vā iti na ca yāvat viśeṣa bādhe tad bidhitam paramparā sādhana tve abādhāt iti mā evam yogya tā hi sva bādhaka pramāvirahaḥ vā sakala bādhaka pramāvirahaḥ vā ādye vahninā siñcati ityādau sva bādhaka pramāta dvirahau samaya bhedena sta iti tad eva yogyam ayogyañca iti prāptam dvitīye tu yogyā anupalabdhā tad niścayaḥ  aśakyaḥ para pramāyā ayogya tvāt  na ca vācyam sakala bādhaka pramāvirahar  svarūpa san  ā iva prayojaka iti ayogye yogya tāmramādanvaya bodha abhāva prasaṅgāt  anyasya tatra bādhaka pramā sattvāt  anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvena bādhaka pramāvirahaḥ niścīyate iti ced  tarhi prāthamika tvāt  sā eva yogya tā na ca sā prakṛte sambhavati iti uktam kiñca eka viśeṣa bādhe śābda sāmānya jñānam tad itara viśeṣa prakāra tā niyatam chidra bādhe chidra itara ghaṭa jñānavat na ca dvāra anupasthityā prakṛte tathā ghaṭate etena yad uktam praśasta rūpavān caitra iti atra gaura śyāma viśeṣān avagame api rūpa mātram avagamyate tadvat  viśeṣān avagame api sādhanatva mātram iti tad pratyuktam tatra eka viśeṣa bādhā bhāvena audāsīni asambhavāt  etena svarga kāma anvaya balāt kriyāyāḥ phala sādhana tvam tad balāt ca paṭoḥ saṃskāsya iva sthāyi tvam kalpyatām kim apūrveṇa saṅkalpa viśeṣasya yāgasya agre pratyakṣa anupalabdhi rātma viśeṣa guṇānām prathama kṣaṇa eva sva viṣayaka pratyakṣa janana svabhāvāt astu na ca evam kriyā antaram api tathā pramāṇa abhāvāt  evam loka prasiddha kriyā kāryatva vyutpattiḥ api bhagnā na bhavati iti parāḥ tam svarga sādhana tā yogya tayā svarga kāma anvayaḥ tad anvaye ca sthāyi tvam iti anyonya āśrayāt lāke dharmi grāhaka mānena kriyāyāḥ kṣaṇikatva niścayāt ca nanu deva pūjā arthaḥ  yajiḥ pūjā ca āra adhanā gauravita prīti hetuḥ kriyā atas  devatā prīti dvārā yāgasya svarga sādhana tvam prīteḥ kṣaṇika tve api prīti anubhava janita saṃskāra dvārā tad sambhavāt ata eva āgneya ādau prīti bhāgitayā agna gaderuddheśya tvam iti ced  na yaj deva pūjāyām iti hi śābdika smṛtiḥ smṛti tvāt eva na svatas  pramāṇam na ca yāgasya devatā prīti hetu tve svargasya devatā prīti sādhya tve vā māna antaram asti vastutas tu cetane deve mānam eva na asti yatra ca viṣṇu prīti kām ādi vādaḥ  asti tatra viṣṇuḥ eva prītiḥ na tu viṣṇoḥ ṣaṣṭhī artha lakṣaṇā doṣāt  viṣṇu śabdasya prīti viśeṣa vācaka tvam veda eva kalpyate na ca devatā pūjā artha yaji anvaya balāt tathā anyonya āśrayāt nanu evam āgneyān dīnām ṣaṇām kṣaṇika tvāt  yogyatā anavagatau parama apūrva kāraṇatva anavagame katham apūrva kalpanā iti ced  na kāmye apūrva vācyatva sthitau āgneya ādau tad vārā sādhana tvasya yogyatā sambhavāt na tu prathamam nanu yaḥ  brāhmaṇāya avaguret tam śatena yātayet iti atra brāhmaṇa badha udyam asya śata yātanā hetutva avagame yathā durita apūrvam kalpyate tathā iha api iti ced  na avaguret  yātayet  iti atra hetu hetumatorliṅiti anuśāsanāt liṅgā avagoraṇa śata yā tanayoṃ  niyatam paurvāparyam bodhyate pratyakṣeṇa anubhava smaraṇayoḥ iva tad ca sādhana tve sādhana sādhana tve vā ubhayam api madhya varti ghaṭitam iti dūrita kalpanam saṃskāravat  iha tu vidhi anuśiṣṭā liṅg kārya tām āha kiñca kāmī kāmyāt anyat  kāmya avyavahita sādhana tayā jñātam eva kartavya tayā avaitī iti niyamāt  na kriyāyām kāminā unvayaḥ  yogyaḥ na ca tṛpti kām asya pāke pravṛtteḥ vyabhicāraḥ odana kāmasya tatra pravṛtteḥ tṛpti kāmanā tu tad kāmanā upayoginaḥ  na tu sākṣāt  anyathā sādhana sādhane pravṛttiḥ na syāt  kāmya sādhana tvam pravartakam lāghavāt iti ced  na bhojana kāmasya siddhaudanasya pāke pravṛtti prasaṅgāt  tasya odana dvārā bhojana sādhanatva aviśeṣāt viśeṣaṇe tu yatra avyavahita sādhanam pākaḥ tad  na kāmyam yad ca kāmyam tatra na avyavahita sādhanam pāka eti na pravṛttiḥ nanu pākasya siddha odana dvārā bhojana sādhana tvam na sambhavati dvārasya asādhya tvāt  odana antara dvārā ca tathā pratisandhāne avyavahita viśeṣaṇe api kutaḥ na pāke pravartate odana antare dvāre sākṣāt sādhana tvāt iti ced  na pākasya bhojana sādhana tve viśeṣasya aprayojaka tayā odana mātrasya dvāra tvāt  tasya ca sādhya tvau  iva ādāt odana viśeṣe ca siddhe odana kāmanā virahāt na tulya tvam nanu odane siddha tvāt  yathā na kāmanā tatas  eva dvāra tā api na atha odana antarasya asiddha tvam ādāya dvāra tā tarhi kāmanā api syāt  tasya asiddha tvam ādāya dvāra tā tarhi kāmanā api syāt  tasya asiddha tvāt iti ced  na pākasya eka viśeṣa dvāra tā bādhaḥ  na viśeṣa antara dvāra tā virodhī sakala viśeṣasya ekatra dvāratva asambhavāt  eka viśeṣa siddhau tu tanmātra kāmanā vicchidyate na hi sakala viśeṣa siddha tvena sāmānya kāmanā vicchedaḥ sakala viśeṣa siddheḥ asambhavena tad anuccheda prasaṅgāt  atha vā kāmyāt anyat  sākṣāt asādhana tvena jñāyamānam yad kartavya tayā kāmaḥ  budhyate tad kāmya avyavahita sādhanam antarā kṛtvā eva yad vā kāmyāt anyat  kāmaḥ  prathamam kāmya avyavahita sādhanam kartavya tayā avaiti paścāt  tad vārā avyavahita sādhanam iti prathamam yāge kāmi kārya tā bodhaḥ  ayogya tā aparāhata eva uttānāḥ tu vivāda viṣayaḥ liṅg samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvita kārya tā ābodhikā pramāṇa liṅga tvāt  laukika liṅgavat  liṅgapa sthāpyam kāryatvam samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvitam liṅupa sthāpi kāryatva tvāt paceta iti kāryatvavat yāgaḥ  vā kāryatva anvitaḥ kriyā kāryatva avagamena apūrvam kalpyam iti tatra prathame yāga anvita kāryatva bodhika tvam liṅgaḥ  bodhyate na tu kriyate na ca yogya tā jñānam vinā tad sambhavati iti uktam eva na hi yogyatā ādikam vinā eva tad anumāna prāmāṇya prayojana mātrāt anvitam abhidhīyate śabdena na antyau kuryāt iti atra vyabhicārāt  veda asya anuvādaka tāpātāt ca nanu apūrve vyutpatti virahaḥ tathā hi prasiddhārtha svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāni atha anupapattyā upasthite śaktiḥ grahītavyā na ca śābda anubhavāt pūrvam apūrvam upasthitam māna abhāvāt apūrvatva vyāghātāt avācyatva apātāt ca na ca liṅga ādinā tad upasthitiḥ vyutpatti anantaram tad pravṛttau  anyonya āśrayāt na ca kāryatvena upalakṣite tatra śakti grahaḥ upalakṣaṇam hi smaraṇam anumānam vā agṛhīte sambandha āgrahāt aśakyam iti mā evam kārye dharmiṇi kāryatvena śakti grahāt  kāryatva viśiṣṭañca upasthitam eva tatas  anvita abhidhāna daśāyām yāga viṣaya kam kāryam iti anubhavaḥ svarga kāma anvayā yogya tayā ghaṭa ādikam tiraskṛtya kriyāṃbhinne yogya tā vaśāt yāga viṣayaka apūrve paryavasyati na tu apūrva tvena śakti grahaḥ na ca apūrvam kāryam iti anubhavaḥ bhavati ca sāmānyatas  sambandha buddhiḥ sahakāri vaśāt  viśeṣa buddhyā payaḥ yathā tava eva kartṛ viśeṣa siddhiḥ nanu kāryatvena api kim ghaṭa ādau śakti grahaḥ uta apūrve ubhayatra vā na ādyaḥ anya pratipattau  anya śakti grahān upayogāt na antyau prāc anupasthiteḥ iti ced  na yena hi rūpeṇa śabdena anubhavaḥ  janyate tena rūpeṇa śakti grahaḥ padārtha smaraṇañca śābda anubhava hetuḥ na hi prameya tvena śakti grahaḥ padārtha smaraṇañca ghaṭa tvena śābda anubhava hetuḥ evañca ghaṭa ādau  eva kārye śaktā liṅgiti śakti grahaḥ tatas  kāryam iti smaraṇam tatas  yogyatā ādi vaśāt pracura dravya guṇa karmāṇi kāryāṇi vihāya yāga viṣaya kam kāryam iti unubhavaḥ  bhavan  apūrvam ālambate yogya tvāt ca tasya sthāyitva lābhaḥ ata eva vākya artha anubhava mātra viṣaya tvāt tad apūrvam na ca smṛtānām ākāṅka ādi vaśāt anvaya bodhaḥ padena kriyate na ca apūrvam smṛti gocara iti vācyam śakti graha padārtha smṛti śābda anubhavānām samāna prakāraka tā mātreṇa hetu hetumat bhāva avadhāraṇāt lāghavāt āvaśyaka tvāt ca na tu kvacid  sahacāra mātreṇa anvaya pratiyogina eva upasthitiḥ tathā gauravāt  gaḥ padāt apūrva gavān anubhava prasaṅgāt ca viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya bodhe sarvatra tathā eva anyathā parvatīya vahniḥ vyāpaka tayā na avagata iti katham tad anvayaḥ  anumitau nanu sāmānya lakṣaṇā pratyāsattyā sarvā eva vyaktayaḥ vyāpti grahe śakti grahe ca viṣayībhavanti katham anyathā parvatīya dhūma vyāpti agrahe tasmāt anumitiḥ iti ced  na yena rūpeṇa vyāpti grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa vyāpya tvena vā pakṣa dharma tā āgrahaḥ  anumitau kāraṇam astu kim tathā api ca sā yadi asti mama api na asti cetāvāpi kiñca tava darśane sā asti iti sutarām apūrva vācya tā kāryatvena hi rūpeṇa apūrvasya api śakti graha viṣaya tvam padārtha smṛti viṣaya tvañca na ca evam apūrvatva kṣatiḥ yāga viṣayatva ādeḥ viśeṣasya kārye liṅgam vinā anupasthiteḥ yathā parvatīyatva bhānam vahnau na anumitim vinā nanu kārye yadi kriyā sādhāraṇena liṅga śaktiḥ kriyā ca ayogya iti yogya pūrva lābhaḥ tadā nitya niṣedha apūrvayoḥ alābhaḥ na hi tatra ayogya tayā kriyā tyaktum śakyate phala aśravaṇāt kalpanāyāñca bīja abhāvāt na ca ekatra nirṇītaḥ śāstrarthaḥ  anyatra tathā eva iti nyāyāt  tatra api apūrvam eva liṅgartha iti tyaktum na hi apūrva tvena śakti grahaḥ kintu kāryatva viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi kriyā ca tathā bhavati eva na ca kāryeṇa samam kriyāyāḥ  anvaya anupapattyā apūrve paryavasānam abhedasya api anvayāt iti mā evam na hi loke paceta iti ādau kārye dharmiṇi śaktiḥ kalpitā kintvananī alabhye kṛti rūpe kāryatva mātre dharmiṇaḥ pāka ādeḥ dhātoḥ eva upasthiti sambhavāt  kriyā kāryatvasya anvitā abhidhāna labhya tvā tathā ca dharmiṇi vede śaktiḥ kalpanīyā sā ca kriyā nirāsena eva na hi kriyāyāḥ kāryatva anvaya yogya tve dharmiṇi śaktiḥ kalpayitum śakyate tasmāt ayogya tayā kriyā nirāsa anantaram tad atirikta eva śaktiḥ kalpanīyā na ca kriyā atirikta kāryāt kārya mātram laghuḥ tatas  kriyā api śakyā eva iti vācyam yatas  na brūmaḥ kriyā atirikta kārya tvena śaktiḥ kintva yogya tayā kriyāyām nirastāyām dharmiṇi śakti kalpana samaye yad  kriyā atiriktam tatra śaktiḥ na tu śakti grahe kriyā praveśaḥ na hi yad prayukta anupapattyā yad kalpanam tad eva tasya viṣayaḥ evañca kāryatvena api tad atirikta kārye eva śakti kalpanāt nitya niṣedhayoḥ api tad eva upāsana ādi anvaya yogyam liṅga abhidhīyate na tu kāryatva mātram dharmiṇi bādhaka abhāvāt lakṣaṇa aprasaṅgāt ca ghaṭa ādiḥ tu liṅga śakti grahe na tiraskriyate na puraskriyate uyayathā api gauravāt  anvita abhidhāna daśāya anvayogyatayā tasya apraveśaḥ vidhi pratyayasya ca tatra aprayogaḥ kevalasya tasya asādhu tvāt dhātu samabhivyāhāra sthale ca tad arthena anvaya bodha janana niyamena ghaṭa ādi apratipādaka tvāt  ata eva aprayogāt eva aprayogaḥ  apūrva tvam vā prayoga upādhiḥ iti vadanti atha apratipādya dhaṭa ādi vṛtti tayā na kāryatvam pravṛtti nimittam pratipādya ghaṭa ādi vṛtti tayā na kāryatvam pravṛtti nimittam pratipādya mātra vṛtteḥ eva tathā tvāt  anyathā prameya tvam eva tathā astu iti ced  na yad prakārikā hi pratipattiḥ pada janyā tad eva tatra pravṛtti nimittam phala kalpya tvāt śakteḥ na tu pratipādya mātra vṛtti sāsnādau vyabhicārāt  na ca prameya tvam tathā tad bodhasya apravartaka tvāt  ata eva lāke liṅg lākṣaṇikaḥ  kriyā bhinne dharmiṇi vede śakti kalpanāt  na ca laukikānām apūrve tātparyam sambhavati pūrvam pramāṇa antareṇa apratīte kriyā sādhāraṇa śaktau  api loke lakṣaṇā eva paceta iti atra hi pāka kārya tā avagamyate tatra kāryatve liṅgaḥ tātparyam lāghavāt  na dharmiṇi kriyāyāḥ  dhātu labhya tvāt  tad āhuḥ tātparyāt hi vṛttiḥ na tu vṛtteḥ tātparyam iti tṛtīyāyāḥ karaṇatva eka tvāt  kāryam kāryatvañca na svatantram śakyam kintu viśiṣṭam viśiṣṭāt ca viśeṣaṇam anyat eva iti kāryatve lakṣaṇā na ca kāryatva viśiṣṭa dharmī upasthitau  api dharmī aṃśam apahāya kriyāyām kāryatva anvayaḥ  astu kim lakṣaṇayā iti vācyam na hi itara dharmi gata tvena upasthitasya dharmi antarākāṅkā asti atas  svatantra kāryatva upasthitaye dharmi antara ākāṅkṣā asti atas  svatantra kāryatva upasthitaye lakṣaṇā yathā puroḍāśa kapālena tuṣa anupapacati iti atra puroḍā śarthitayā tad anvita tvena upasthitasya kapālasya na upavāpa ākāṅkṣa iti svatantra kapāla upasthitaye adhiṣṭhāna lakṣaṇā na ca vyutpatti virodhaḥ na hi loke kriyā kārya tve śaktiḥ avadhāritā yena virodhaḥ  bhavet  kintu kāryatva mātre kriyāyāḥ  dhātu labhya tvāt  na ca dharmi antare śaktau  api tad bhaṅgaḥ tasmāt  prakṛti artha anvita sva artha bodhaka tvam pratyayānām gṛhītam pratyaya arthaḥ ca apūrvam api iti na virodhaḥ astu vā loke liṅgaḥ kriyā kārya tve śaktiḥ tathā api tad bhaṅgam vinā eva nānā artha nyāyena vede dharmi antare śaktiḥ tām vinā svarga kāma anvaya asambhavāt  anye tu paceta iti ādau dhātunā eva pākaḥ kāryaḥ  abhidhīyate liṅg tatra tātparyagrāhikā na tu śaktā niyamataḥ tādṛśi eva tad prayogāt  sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣa paratvañca na vṛtti antara nirvāhyam ata eva vartamānatva ādau na laṅgā ādi śaktiḥ iti loke śakya grahāt  na vyutpatti virodha iti tad asat  liṅaḥ kāryatve aśaktau pacipadāt  kāryatva jñāna anupapatteḥ yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhāt na ca ajahatsva arthā ubhaya sādhāraṇasya anupasthiteḥ iti diś  yad vā jñāne padānām śaktiḥ śakya tvāt  evañca liṅga padam ekatra uccāraṇe yogyatā ādi vaśāt yāga viṣaya kam stāyi svarga janakam kāryam iti ekam jñānam anubhava rūpam pracura dravya guṇa karma vilakṣaṇa viṣayam kriyate na ca evam nānā arthavat ekaika jñāne śakti grahāt eka eka viṣayaḥ  anubhavaḥ  bhavet  na samudita viṣaya iti vācyam śakti graha kāle ekatra uccāraṇa iti viśeṣaṇa mahimnā tad sambhavāt nānā arthe tu pramāṇa abhāvena gauravena ca śakti grahe tasya apraveśanāt tathā api amīṣām samūha ālambanam syāt na tu parasparam vaiśiṣṭya jñānam iti ced  na sā kāṅkṣa dharma dharmi gocara eka jñānasya eva viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt  cana ca samūha ālambana sambhedaḥ tasya nirākāṅkṣa viṣaya tvāt  astu vā upasthiteṣṭha gṛhīta asaṃsargeṣu sthāyitva svarga janakatva kāryatveṣu śaktiḥ agṛhīta asaṃsargakasya api viśiṣṭa jñāna samāna śīla tvāt  ata ukta nyāyena tāvat viṣayakam ekam jñānam liṅgpadena janyate evam eva alaukika artheṣu svarga ādi padeṣu śakti grahaḥ nanu bhavatu ukta prakāreṇa śaktigrahaḥ tathā api liṅpadāt  yāga viṣayaka kārya anubhave satya pūrva lābhāt svarga kāma anvayaḥ sambhavati iti upapādaka pratisandhāne prasiddhārtha svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāni atha anupapattyā liṅgaḥ kārye śakti kalpanam na hi prathamam upapādaka pratisandhānam vinā artha āpattiḥ sambhavati na ca śakti kalpanāt  pūrvam upapādaka śarīra niviṣṭam apūrvam jñātam iti ced  tad  kim ya eva viśeṣa upapādakaḥ pakṣa dharma tā balāt siddhyati tad pratisandhānam artha āpattau kāraṇam tathā tve pūrvam gṛhīta mātrasya kalpyate kalpanā uccheda āpattiḥ tasmāt  yathā sāmānya tobhojanasya pīnatva sambandha avagamāt  upapādaka tarke sati kalpanātaḥ  viśeṣa avagamaḥ yathā vā sāmānya śakta vyakti vācaka padena samabhivyāhāra vaśāt viśeṣa abhidhānam evam atra api kārya mātra vācaka tve kārya viśeṣa lābhaḥ sambhavati iti tarkita upapādaka pratisandhānāt  bhavati artha āpattyā śakti kalpanam yāga viṣaya kañca kāryam na ghaṭa ādi tasya sa viṣaya katva abhāvāt viṣaya tvañca jñāna ghaṭayoḥ iva svabhāva sambandhaḥ vā tad nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvam vā tad sāna saṃvita saṃvedya tvam vā vyāvṛtta sādhana tvam vā iti asti hi yāga dāna homa janyā pūrvāṇām tulya rūpa sādhana antara vyavacchedena pratyeka mātra janya tvam tad uktam viśabdaḥ  hi viśeṣa arthaḥ sinotiḥ bandha ucyate viśeṣeṇa sinoti iti viṣayaḥ  atas  niyāmakaḥ iti nanu yena rūpeṇa śakti grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa kāryatva śakta āliṅg padāt lakṣaṇayā kārya upasthitau yogyatā ādi vaśāt apūrva lābhaḥ  astu kārya smaraṇam hi anvita abhidhāna upayogi na tu apūrva smaraṇam tad ca padena padārthena vā iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ kāryañca śakya kāryatva sambandhi tayā avagatam eva iti ced  na liṅgaḥ  lākṣaṇika tvena apūrva ananubhāvaka tvāt  na ca itara anvitasva artha śaktasya yajya ādi padasya itarat pūrvam ādāya anubhāvaka tvam iti vācyam itara upalakṣita sva artha anvaya mātre hi padānām śaktiḥ na tu itaratra gauravāt  pada antara labhya tvāt ca lakṣaṇa āya añca tīra upalakṣita anvaya śāli sva artha anubhāvaka tvīm itarapadasya tīrasya tu saṃskārāt upasthitiḥ asat nihitena anvita abhidhāna abhāvāt na ca apūrvam saṃskāra viṣayaḥ kiñca yajipadena svarga kāma kārya viṣayaḥ  yāga iti unubhava ubhavet  lakṣaṇāyām itara padasya lakṣaṇīya viśeṣaṇa sva artha viśeṣyaka anubhava janaka tvāt  na ca etādṛśaḥ  bodha ākāṅkṣitaḥ na ca yāga aviśeṣita kārya mātreṇa svarga kāma anvayaḥ pratīyate kintu yāga viṣayaka kārya viśeṣe tathā ca tathāvidha bodha artham liṅgaḥ kārye śaktiḥ eva iti apūrvavāda siddhāntaḥ atra ucyate anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvam na yogya tā anāpta ukte payasā siñcati iti atra sati api anvaya prayojaka drava dravya tve bādhaka pramāyām anvaya ābodhāt  atha yogya tve api sva bādhaka pramāyām anvayā bodhāt atha yogya tve api sva bādhaka pramāvirahar  kāraṇam tarhi saḥ  api avaśya apekṣaṇīyā eti lāghavāt  sā eva yogya tā evañca tad eva yogyam ayogyañca syāt iti ced  satyam yathā daśā viśeṣe tad eva sā kāṅkṣam anākāṅkṣam āsannañca tathā sva bādhaka pramāta dvirahadaśāyām tad eva anvaya bodhe yogyam ayogyañcā abhidhīyate sva bādhaka pramāyām tad virahe vā yogya ayogya tā vyavahāra darśanāt sva bādhaka pramāvira hadaśāyām yogyatā ādi sattve api vahninā siñcati iti atra anvaya bodhaḥ apramā doṣavat puruṣaṇīta tvāt sāmānya bhānasya kiñcid viśeṣa bhāna niyata tvāt viśeṣa ābhāne katham tad bhāsata iti na vastu gatyā paramparā sādhanam viśeṣaḥ  bhāsata evaya paramparā sādhanatvantu prakāraḥ  na bhāsate tad prakāra bhāne hi paramparā ghaṭaka jñānasya hetu tvāt  yathā ghaṭena jalam āhara iti atra yogyatayā chidra itara ghaṭe ghaṭa tvena bhāsate na tu chidretara tvena tathā sati lakṣaṇāyām yugapad  vṛtti dvaya virodhena ghaṭān anvaya prasaṅgāt  ubhaya sādhāraṇa rūpeṇa anupasthiteḥ ca na ajahatsva arthā atha saṃskārāt tad u sthitiḥ na ca subvibhaktīnām prakṛti artha gata sva artha anvaya bodhakatva vyutpatteḥ tatra vibhakti arthaḥ  na avyīyeta iti vācyam prakṛti arthaḥ  hi prakṛti pratipādyāḥ lakṣaṇīya anvaya anurodhāt  sa ca saṃskāra sahakārāt  prakṛte api na ca tasya aniyata udbodhakān na niyatā tad upasthitiḥ phala balena tathā kalpanāt iti ced  na śabda upasthā api tana eva śabdasya anvaya bodhaka tvāt na ca evam ākāśa pada aśakyasya saṃskāra upasthitasya śabda āśraya tvasya katham śābda anubhava viṣaya tvam iti vācyam niyamataḥ  yad dharmavat tvena upasthite yatra śakti grahaḥ tad smaraṇa janaka saṃskārasya tad dharma viṣaya tā niyamena tad udbodhakāt eva tad aṃśe api udbodha niyamena ākāśa padāt aśakyasya api tasya bhānāt  astu vā tad api śakyam yadi niyamata upasthitiḥ saha prayogasya vāci ādi paratvena api upapatteḥ vastutas tu niyata upasthitiḥ eva na asti astu vā padāt api nirvikalpakam tarhi anvaya bodha daśāyām itara anvaya an upapatti abhāvāt agrre api kalpanā na syāt iti ced  tarhi tava api kārya tā bodha anantaram aupādānikam ādhana tā bodhaḥ  na syāt  aupādānikam ādhana tā bodhaḥ  na syāt  aupādānika bodhe anupapatti bodhasya hetu tvāt  klapanā mātra ucchedaḥ ca evam syāt  pratīta anupapatti mūla tvāt kalpanāyāḥ vastutas tu bādhaka pramā virahasya yogyatā tve saṃśaya pasādhāraṇam jñāna mātram eva tasyāḥ prayojakam tena yatra bādhaka pramāniḥ cayaḥ tatra eva anvaya bodha abhāvaḥ  anyatra tu tad dhīmātrāt śabda bodha iti yāge api yogyatā saṃśayena anvaya bodha apratibandhaḥ bādha saṃśayasya apratibandhaka tvāt  anyathā anumāna ādi uccheda prasaṅgāt  apūrva vācya tve api apūrve svarga sādhana tā saṃśayāt yogyatāyāḥ saṃśaya eva apūrvasya prathamam svarga sādhana tvā niḥ cayāt upādānasya anvita abhidhāna uttara kālīna tvāt sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvena dvāra sambhavanayā sādhanatva sambhā avanātaḥ svarga kāma anvaya iti tulyam api ca yathā na kriyā sthirā iti ayoṅgyā tathā kāryam apūrvam api viśiṣṭam na sthiram kṛteḥ vinaṣṭa tvāt  na ca adhiṣeṭhāne apūrva mātre sādhana tvam tasya pada ārya eka deśa tvena anvaya apratiyogi tvāt anye tu anvaya virodhi rūpa virahaḥ  yogya tā ata eva vahninā siñcati iti atra tad  bhrame bhavati anvaya bhramaḥ yāge ca anvaya virodhi rūpa virahaḥ  yogyā anupalabdhyā sugama eva na
